agre bR^ihannuShasAmUrdhvo asthAnnirjaganvAntamaso jyotiShAgAt |agnirbhAnunA rushatA sva~Nga A jAto vishvA sadmAnyaprAH || 10.1.1
sa jAto garbho asi rodasyoragne chArurvibhR^ita oShadhIShu |chitraH shishuH pari tamAMsyaktUnpra mAtR^ibhyo adhi kanikradadgAH || 10.1.2
viShNuritthA paramamasya vidvA~njAto bR^ihannabhi pAti tR^itIyam |AsA yadasya payo akrata svaM sachetaso abhyarchantyatra || 10.1.3
ata u tvA pitubhR^ito janitrIrannAvR^idhaM prati charantyannaiH |tA IM pratyeShi punaranyarUpA asi tvaM vikShu mAnuShIShu hotA || 10.1.4
hotAraM chitrarathamadhvarasya yaj~nasyayaj~nasya ketuM rushantam |pratyardhiM devasyadevasya mahnA shriyA tvagnimatithiM janAnAm || 10.1.5
sa tu vastrANyadha peshanAni vasAno agnirnAbhA pR^ithivyAH |aruSho jAtaH pada iLAyAH purohito rAjanyakShIha devAn || 10.1.6
A hi dyAvApR^ithivI agna ubhe sadA putro na mAtarA tatantha |pra yAhyachChoshato yaviShThAthA vaha sahasyeha devAn || 10.1.7

piprIhi devA.N ushato yaviShTha vidvA.N R^itU.NrR^itupate yajeha |ye daivyA R^itvijastebhiragne tvaM hotR^INAmasyAyajiShThaH || 10.2.1
veShi hotramuta potraM janAnAM mandhAtAsi draviNodA R^itAvA |svAhA vayaM kR^iNavAmA havIMShi devo devAnyajatvagnirarhan || 10.2.2
A devAnAmapi panthAmaganma yachChaknavAma tadanu pravoLhum |agnirvidvAnsa yajAtsedu hotA so adhvarAnsa R^itUnkalpayAti || 10.2.3
yadvo vayaM praminAma vratAni viduShAM devA aviduShTarAsaH |agniShTadvishvamA pR^iNAti vidvAnyebhirdevA.N R^itubhiH kalpayAti || 10.2.4
yatpAkatrA manasA dInadakShA na yaj~nasya manvate martyAsaH |agniShTaddhotA kratuvidvijAnanyajiShTho devA.N R^itusho yajAti || 10.2.5
vishveShAM hyadhvarANAmanIkaM chitraM ketuM janitA tvA jajAna |sa A yajasva nR^ivatIranu kShAH spArhA iShaH kShumatIrvishvajanyAH || 10.2.6
yaM tvA dyAvApR^ithivI yaM tvApastvaShTA yaM tvA sujanimA jajAna |panthAmanu pravidvAnpitR^iyANaM dyumadagne samidhAno vi bhAhi || 10.2.7

ino rAjannaratiH samiddho raudro dakShAya suShumA.N adarshi |chikidvi bhAti bhAsA bR^ihatAsiknImeti rushatImapAjan || 10.3.1
kR^iShNAM yadenImabhi varpasA bhUjjanayanyoShAM bR^ihataH piturjAm |UrdhvaM bhAnuM sUryasya stabhAyandivo vasubhiraratirvi bhAti || 10.3.2
bhadro bhadrayA sachamAna AgAtsvasAraM jAro abhyeti pashchAt |supraketairdyubhiragnirvitiShThanrushadbhirvarNairabhi rAmamasthAt || 10.3.3
asya yAmAso bR^ihato na vagnUnindhAnA agneH sakhyuH shivasya |IDyasya vR^iShNo bR^ihataH svAso bhAmAso yAmannaktavashchikitre || 10.3.4
svanA na yasya bhAmAsaH pavante rochamAnasya bR^ihataH sudivaH |jyeShThebhiryastejiShThaiH krILumadbhirvarShiShThebhirbhAnubhirnakShati dyAm || 10.3.5
asya shuShmAso dadR^ishAnapaverjehamAnasya svanayanniyudbhiH |pratnebhiryo rushadbhirdevatamo vi rebhadbhiraratirbhAti vibhvA || 10.3.6
sa A vakShi mahi na A cha satsi divaspR^ithivyoraratiryuvatyoH |agniH sutukaH sutukebhirashvai rabhasvadbhI rabhasvA.N eha gamyAH || 10.3.7

pra te yakShi pra ta iyarmi manma bhuvo yathA vandyo no haveShu |dhanvanniva prapA asi tvamagna iyakShave pUrave pratna rAjan || 10.4.1
yaM tvA janAso abhi saMcharanti gAva uShNamiva vrajaM yaviShTha |dUto devAnAmasi martyAnAmantarmahA.Nshcharasi rochanena || 10.4.2
shishuM na tvA jenyaM vardhayantI mAtA bibharti sachanasyamAnA |dhanoradhi pravatA yAsi harya~njigIShase pashurivAvasR^iShTaH || 10.4.3
mUrA amUra na vayaM chikitvo mahitvamagne tvama~Nga vitse |shaye vavrishcharati jihvayAdanrerihyate yuvatiM vishpatiH san || 10.4.4
kUchijjAyate sanayAsu navyo vane tasthau palito dhUmaketuH |asnAtApo vR^iShabho na pra veti sachetaso yaM praNayanta martAH || 10.4.5
tanUtyajeva taskarA vanargU rashanAbhirdashabhirabhyadhItAm |iyaM te agne navyasI manIShA yukShvA rathaM na shuchayadbhira~NgaiH || 10.4.6
brahma cha te jAtavedo namashcheyaM cha gIH sadamidvardhanI bhUt |rakShA No agne tanayAni tokA rakShota nastanvo aprayuchChan || 10.4.7

ekaH samudro dharuNo rayINAmasmaddhR^ido bhUrijanmA vi chaShTe |siShaktyUdharniNyorupastha utsasya madhye nihitaM padaM veH || 10.5.1
samAnaM nILaM vR^iShaNo vasAnAH saM jagmire mahiShA arvatIbhiH |R^itasya padaM kavayo ni pAnti guhA nAmAni dadhire parANi || 10.5.2
R^itAyinI mAyinI saM dadhAte mitvA shishuM jaj~naturvardhayantI |vishvasya nAbhiM charato dhruvasya kaveshchittantuM manasA viyantaH || 10.5.3
R^itasya hi vartanayaH sujAtamiSho vAjAya pradivaH sachante |adhIvAsaM rodasI vAvasAne ghR^itairannairvAvR^idhAte madhUnAm || 10.5.4
sapta svasR^IraruShIrvAvashAno vidvAnmadhva ujjabhArA dR^ishe kam |antaryeme antarikShe purAjA ichChanvavrimavidatpUShaNasya || 10.5.5
sapta maryAdAH kavayastatakShustAsAmekAmidabhyaMhuro gAt |Ayorha skambha upamasya nILe pathAM visarge dharuNeShu tasthau || 10.5.6
asachcha sachcha parame vyomandakShasya janmannaditerupasthe |agnirha naH prathamajA R^itasya pUrva Ayuni vR^iShabhashcha dhenuH || 10.5.7

ayaM sa yasya sharmannavobhiragneredhate jaritAbhiShTau |jyeShThebhiryo bhAnubhirR^iShUNAM paryeti parivIto vibhAvA || 10.6.1
yo bhAnubhirvibhAvA vibhAtyagnirdevebhirR^itAvAjasraH |A yo vivAya sakhyA sakhibhyo.aparihvR^ito atyo na saptiH || 10.6.2
Ishe yo vishvasyA devavIterIshe vishvAyuruShaso vyuShTau |A yasminmanA havIMShyagnAvariShTarathaH skabhnAti shUShaiH || 10.6.3
shUShebhirvR^idho juShANo arkairdevA.N achChA raghupatvA jigAti |mandro hotA sa juhvA yajiShThaH sammishlo agnirA jigharti devAn || 10.6.4
tamusrAmindraM na rejamAnamagniM gIrbhirnamobhirA kR^iNudhvam |A yaM viprAso matibhirgR^iNanti jAtavedasaM juhvaM sahAnAm || 10.6.5
saM yasminvishvA vasUni jagmurvAje nAshvAH saptIvanta evaiH |asme UtIrindravAtatamA arvAchInA agna A kR^iNuShva || 10.6.6
adhA hyagne mahnA niShadyA sadyo jaj~nAno havyo babhUtha |taM te devAso anu ketamAyannadhAvardhanta prathamAsa UmAH || 10.6.7

svasti no divo agne pR^ithivyA vishvAyurdhehi yajathAya deva |sachemahi tava dasma praketairuruShyA Na urubhirdeva shaMsaiH || 10.7.1
imA agne matayastubhyaM jAtA gobhirashvairabhi gR^iNanti rAdhaH |yadA te marto anu bhogamAnaDvaso dadhAno matibhiH sujAta || 10.7.2
agniM manye pitaramagnimApimagniM bhrAtaraM sadamitsakhAyam |agneranIkaM bR^ihataH saparyaM divi shukraM yajataM sUryasya || 10.7.3
sidhrA agne dhiyo asme sanutrIryaM trAyase dama A nityahotA |R^itAvA sa rohidashvaH purukShurdyubhirasmA ahabhirvAmamastu || 10.7.4
dyubhirhitaM mitramiva prayogaM pratnamR^itvijamadhvarasya jAram |bAhubhyAmagnimAyavo.ajananta vikShu hotAraM nyasAdayanta || 10.7.5
svayaM yajasva divi deva devAnkiM te pAkaH kR^iNavadaprachetAH |yathAyaja R^itubhirdeva devAnevA yajasva tanvaM sujAta || 10.7.6
bhavA no agne.avitota gopA bhavA vayaskR^iduta no vayodhAH |rAsvA cha naH sumaho havyadAtiM trAsvota nastanvo aprayuchChan || 10.7.7

pra ketunA bR^ihatA yAtyagnirA rodasI vR^iShabho roravIti |divashchidantA.N upamA.N udAnaLapAmupasthe mahiSho vavardha || 10.8.1
mumoda garbho vR^iShabhaH kakudmAnasremA vatsaH shimIvA.N arAvIt |sa devatAtyudyatAni kR^iNvansveShu kShayeShu prathamo jigAti || 10.8.2
A yo mUrdhAnaM pitrorarabdha nyadhvare dadhire sUro arNaH |asya patmannaruShIrashvabudhnA R^itasya yonau tanvo juShanta || 10.8.3
uShauSho hi vaso agrameShi tvaM yamayorabhavo vibhAvA |R^itAya sapta dadhiShe padAni janayanmitraM tanve svAyai || 10.8.4
bhuvashchakShurmaha R^itasya gopA bhuvo varuNo yadR^itAya veShi |bhuvo apAM napAjjAtavedo bhuvo dUto yasya havyaM jujoShaH || 10.8.5
bhuvo yaj~nasya rajasashcha netA yatrA niyudbhiH sachase shivAbhiH |divi mUrdhAnaM dadhiShe svarShAM jihvAmagne chakR^iShe havyavAham || 10.8.6
asya tritaH kratunA vavre antarichChandhItiM piturevaiH parasya |sachasyamAnaH pitrorupasthe jAmi bruvANa AyudhAni veti || 10.8.7
sa pitryANyAyudhAni vidvAnindreShita Aptyo abhyayudhyat |trishIrShANaM saptarashmiM jaghanvAntvAShTrasya chinniH sasR^ije trito gAH || 10.8.8
bhUrIdindra udinakShantamojo.avAbhinatsatpatirmanyamAnam |tvAShTrasya chidvishvarUpasya gonAmAchakrANastrINi shIrShA parA vark || 10.8.9

Apo hi ShThA mayobhuvastA na Urje dadhAtana |mahe raNAya chakShase || 10.9.1
yo vaH shivatamo rasastasya bhAjayateha naH |ushatIriva mAtaraH || 10.9.2
tasmA araM gamAma vo yasya kShayAya jinvatha |Apo janayathA cha naH || 10.9.3
shaM no devIrabhiShTaya Apo bhavantu pItaye |shaM yorabhi sravantu naH || 10.9.4
IshAnA vAryANAM kShayantIshcharShaNInAm |apo yAchAmi bheShajam || 10.9.5
apsu me somo abravIdantarvishvAni bheShajA |agniM cha vishvashambhuvam || 10.9.6
ApaH pR^iNIta bheShajaM varUthaM tanve mama |jyokcha sUryaM dR^ishe || 10.9.7
idamApaH pra vahata yatkiM cha duritaM mayi |yadvAhamabhidudroha yadvA shepa utAnR^itam || 10.9.8
Apo adyAnvachAriShaM rasena samagasmahi |payasvAnagna A gahi taM mA saM sR^ija varchasA || 10.9.9

o chitsakhAyaM sakhyA vavR^ityAM tiraH purU chidarNavaM jaganvAn |piturnapAtamA dadhIta vedhA adhi kShami prataraM dIdhyAnaH || 10.10.1
na te sakhA sakhyaM vaShTyetatsalakShmA yadviShurUpA bhavAti |mahasputrAso asurasya vIrA divo dhartAra urviyA pari khyan || 10.10.2
ushanti ghA te amR^itAsa etadekasya chittyajasaM martyasya |ni te mano manasi dhAyyasme janyuH patistanvamA vivishyAH || 10.10.3
na yatpurA chakR^imA kaddha nUnamR^itA vadanto anR^itaM rapema |gandharvo apsvapyA cha yoShA sA no nAbhiH paramaM jAmi tannau || 10.10.4
garbhe nu nau janitA dampatI kardevastvaShTA savitA vishvarUpaH |nakirasya pra minanti vratAni veda nAvasya pR^ithivI uta dyauH || 10.10.5
ko asya veda prathamasyAhnaH ka IM dadarsha ka iha pra vochat |bR^ihanmitrasya varuNasya dhAma kadu brava Ahano vIchyA nR^In || 10.10.6
yamasya mA yamyaM kAma AgansamAne yonau sahasheyyAya |jAyeva patye tanvaM ririchyAM vi chidvR^iheva rathyeva chakrA || 10.10.7
na tiShThanti na ni miShantyete devAnAM spasha iha ye charanti |anyena madAhano yAhi tUyaM tena vi vR^iha rathyeva chakrA || 10.10.8
rAtrIbhirasmA ahabhirdashasyetsUryasya chakShurmuhurunmimIyAt |divA pR^ithivyA mithunA sabandhU yamIryamasya bibhR^iyAdajAmi || 10.10.9
A ghA tA gachChAnuttarA yugAni yatra jAmayaH kR^iNavannajAmi |upa barbR^ihi vR^iShabhAya bAhumanyamichChasva subhage patiM mat || 10.10.10
kiM bhrAtAsadyadanAthaM bhavAti kimu svasA yannirR^itirnigachChAt |kAmamUtA bahvetadrapAmi tanvA me tanvaM saM pipR^igdhi || 10.10.11
na vA u te tanvA tanvaM saM papR^ichyAM pApamAhuryaH svasAraM nigachChAt |anyena matpramudaH kalpayasva na te bhrAtA subhage vaShTyetat || 10.10.12
bato batAsi yama naiva te mano hR^idayaM chAvidAma |anyA kila tvAM kakShyeva yuktaM pari ShvajAte libujeva vR^ikSham || 10.10.13
anyamU Shu tvaM yamyanya u tvAM pari ShvajAte libujeva vR^ikSham |tasya vA tvaM mana ichChA sa vA tavAdhA kR^iNuShva saMvidaM subhadrAm || 10.10.14

vR^iShA vR^iShNe duduhe dohasA divaH payAMsi yahvo aditeradAbhyaH |vishvaM sa veda varuNo yathA dhiyA sa yaj~niyo yajatu yaj~niyA.N R^itUn || 10.11.1
rapadgandharvIrapyA cha yoShaNA nadasya nAde pari pAtu me manaH |iShTasya madhye aditirni dhAtu no bhrAtA no jyeShThaH prathamo vi vochati || 10.11.2
so chinnu bhadrA kShumatI yashasvatyuShA uvAsa manave svarvatI |yadImushantamushatAmanu kratumagniM hotAraM vidathAya jIjanan || 10.11.3
adha tyaM drapsaM vibhvaM vichakShaNaM virAbharadiShitaH shyeno adhvare |yadI visho vR^iNate dasmamAryA agniM hotAramadha dhIrajAyata || 10.11.4
sadAsi raNvo yavaseva puShyate hotrAbhiragne manuShaH svadhvaraH |viprasya vA yachChashamAna ukthyaM vAjaM sasavA.N upayAsi bhUribhiH || 10.11.5
udIraya pitarA jAra A bhagamiyakShati haryato hR^itta iShyati |vivakti vahniH svapasyate makhastaviShyate asuro vepate matI || 10.11.6
yaste agne sumatiM marto akShatsahasaH sUno ati sa pra shR^iNve |iShaM dadhAno vahamAno ashvairA sa dyumA.N amavAnbhUShati dyUn || 10.11.7
yadagna eShA samitirbhavAti devI deveShu yajatA yajatra |ratnA cha yadvibhajAsi svadhAvo bhAgaM no atra vasumantaM vItAt || 10.11.8
shrudhI no agne sadane sadhasthe yukShvA rathamamR^itasya dravitnum |A no vaha rodasI devaputre mAkirdevAnAmapa bhUriha syAH || 10.11.9

dyAvA ha kShAmA prathame R^itenAbhishrAve bhavataH satyavAchA |devo yanmartAnyajathAya kR^iNvansIdaddhotA pratya~NsvamasuM yan || 10.12.1
devo devAnparibhUrR^itena vahA no havyaM prathamashchikitvAn |dhUmaketuH samidhA bhAR^ijIko mandro hotA nityo vAchA yajIyAn || 10.12.2
svAvR^igdevasyAmR^itaM yadI gorato jAtAso dhArayanta urvI |vishve devA anu tatte yajurgurduhe yadenI divyaM ghR^itaM vAH || 10.12.3
archAmi vAM vardhAyApo ghR^itasnU dyAvAbhUmI shR^iNutaM rodasI me |ahA yaddyAvo.asunItimayanmadhvA no atra pitarA shishItAm || 10.12.4
kiM svinno rAjA jagR^ihe kadasyAti vrataM chakR^imA ko vi veda |mitrashchiddhi ShmA juhurANo devA~nChloko na yAtAmapi vAjo asti || 10.12.5
durmantvatrAmR^itasya nAma salakShmA yadviShurUpA bhavAti |yamasya yo manavate sumantvagne tamR^iShva pAhyaprayuchChan || 10.12.6
yasmindevA vidathe mAdayante vivasvataH sadane dhArayante |sUrye jyotiradadhurmAsyaktUnpari dyotaniM charato ajasrA || 10.12.7
yasmindevA manmani saMcharantyapIchye na vayamasya vidma |mitro no atrAditiranAgAnsavitA devo varuNAya vochat || 10.12.8
shrudhI no agne sadane sadhasthe yukShvA rathamamR^itasya dravitnum |A no vaha rodasI devaputre mAkirdevAnAmapa bhUriha syAH || 10.12.9

yuje vAM brahma pUrvyaM namobhirvi shloka etu pathyeva sUreH |shR^iNvantu vishve amR^itasya putrA A ye dhAmAni divyAni tasthuH || 10.13.1
yame iva yatamAne yadaitaM pra vAM bharanmAnuShA devayantaH |A sIdataM svamu lokaM vidAne svAsasthe bhavatamindave naH || 10.13.2
pa~ncha padAni rupo anvarohaM chatuShpadImanvemi vratena |akShareNa prati mima etAmR^itasya nAbhAvadhi saM punAmi || 10.13.3
devebhyaH kamavR^iNIta mR^ityuM prajAyai kamamR^itaM nAvR^iNIta |bR^ihaspatiM yaj~namakR^iNvata R^iShiM priyAM yamastanvaM prArirechIt || 10.13.4
sapta kSharanti shishave marutvate pitre putrAso apyavIvatannR^itam |ubhe idasyobhayasya rAjata ubhe yatete ubhayasya puShyataH || 10.13.5

pareyivAMsaM pravato mahIranu bahubhyaH panthAmanupaspashAnam |vaivasvataM saMgamanaM janAnAM yamaM rAjAnaM haviShA duvasya || 10.14.1
yamo no gAtuM prathamo viveda naiShA gavyUtirapabhartavA u |yatrA naH pUrve pitaraH pareyurenA jaj~nAnAH pathyA anu svAH || 10.14.2
mAtalI kavyairyamo a~NgirobhirbR^ihaspatirR^ikvabhirvAvR^idhAnaH |yA.Nshcha devA vAvR^idhurye cha devAnsvAhAnye svadhayAnye madanti || 10.14.3
imaM yama prastaramA hi sIdA~NgirobhiH pitR^ibhiH saMvidAnaH |A tvA mantrAH kavishastA vahantvenA rAjanhaviShA mAdayasva || 10.14.4
a~NgirobhirA gahi yaj~niyebhiryama vairUpairiha mAdayasva |vivasvantaM huve yaH pitA te.asminyaj~ne barhiShyA niShadya || 10.14.5
a~Ngiraso naH pitaro navagvA atharvANo bhR^igavaH somyAsaH |teShAM vayaM sumatau yaj~niyAnAmapi bhadre saumanase syAma || 10.14.6
prehi prehi pathibhiH pUrvyebhiryatrA naH pUrve pitaraH pareyuH |ubhA rAjAnA svadhayA madantA yamaM pashyAsi varuNaM cha devam || 10.14.7
saM gachChasva pitR^ibhiH saM yameneShTApUrtena parame vyoman |hitvAyAvadyaM punarastamehi saM gachChasva tanvA suvarchAH || 10.14.8
apeta vIta vi cha sarpatAto.asmA etaM pitaro lokamakran |ahobhiradbhiraktubhirvyaktaM yamo dadAtyavasAnamasmai || 10.14.9
ati drava sArameyau shvAnau chaturakShau shabalau sAdhunA pathA |athA pitR^InsuvidatrA.N upehi yamena ye sadhamAdaM madanti || 10.14.10
yau te shvAnau yama rakShitArau chaturakShau pathirakShI nR^ichakShasau |tAbhyAmenaM pari dehi rAjansvasti chAsmA anamIvaM cha dhehi || 10.14.11
urUNasAvasutR^ipA udumbalau yamasya dUtau charato janA.N anu |tAvasmabhyaM dR^ishaye sUryAya punardAtAmasumadyeha bhadram || 10.14.12
yamAya somaM sunuta yamAya juhutA haviH |yamaM ha yaj~no gachChatyagnidUto araMkR^itaH || 10.14.13
yamAya ghR^itavaddhavirjuhota pra cha tiShThata |sa no deveShvA yamaddIrghamAyuH pra jIvase || 10.14.14
yamAya madhumattamaM rAj~ne havyaM juhotana |idaM nama R^iShibhyaH pUrvajebhyaH pUrvebhyaH pathikR^idbhyaH || 10.14.15
trikadrukebhiH patati ShaLurvIrekamidbR^ihat |triShTubgAyatrI ChandAMsi sarvA tA yama AhitA || 10.14.16

udIratAmavara utparAsa unmadhyamAH pitaraH somyAsaH |asuM ya IyuravR^ikA R^itaj~nAste no.avantu pitaro haveShu || 10.15.1
idaM pitR^ibhyo namo astvadya ye pUrvAso ya uparAsa IyuH |ye pArthive rajasyA niShattA ye vA nUnaM suvR^ijanAsu vikShu || 10.15.2
AhaM pitR^InsuvidatrA.N avitsi napAtaM cha vikramaNaM cha viShNoH |barhiShado ye svadhayA sutasya bhajanta pitvasta ihAgamiShThAH || 10.15.3
barhiShadaH pitara UtyarvAgimA vo havyA chakR^imA juShadhvam |ta A gatAvasA shaMtamenAthA naH shaM yorarapo dadhAta || 10.15.4
upahUtAH pitaraH somyAso barhiShyeShu nidhiShu priyeShu |ta A gamantu ta iha shruvantvadhi bruvantu te.avantvasmAn || 10.15.5
AchyA jAnu dakShiNato niShadyemaM yaj~namabhi gR^iNIta vishve |mA hiMsiShTa pitaraH kena chinno yadva AgaH puruShatA karAma || 10.15.6
AsInAso aruNInAmupasthe rayiM dhatta dAshuShe martyAya |putrebhyaH pitarastasya vasvaH pra yachChata ta ihorjaM dadhAta || 10.15.7

ye tAtR^iShurdevatrA jehamAnA hotrAvidaH stomataShTAso arkaiH |Agne yAhi suvidatrebhirarvA~NsatyaiH kavyaiH pitR^ibhirgharmasadbhiH || 10.15.9
ye satyAso havirado haviShpA indreNa devaiH sarathaM dadhAnAH |Agne yAhi sahasraM devavandaiH paraiH pUrvaiH pitR^ibhirgharmasadbhiH || 10.15.10
agniShvAttAH pitara eha gachChata sadaHsadaH sadata supraNItayaH |attA havIMShi prayatAni barhiShyathA rayiM sarvavIraM dadhAtana || 10.15.11

mainamagne vi daho mAbhi shocho mAsya tvachaM chikShipo mA sharIram |yadA shR^itaM kR^iNavo jAtavedo.athemenaM pra hiNutAtpitR^ibhyaH || 10.16.1

tvaShTA duhitre vahatuM kR^iNotItIdaM vishvaM bhuvanaM sameti |yamasya mAtA paryuhyamAnA maho jAyA vivasvato nanAsha || 10.17.1

pUShA tvetashchyAvayatu pra vidvAnanaShTapashurbhuvanasya gopAH |sa tvaitebhyaH pari dadatpitR^ibhyo.agnirdevebhyaH suvidatriyebhyaH || 10.17.3
AyurvishvAyuH pari pAsati tvA pUShA tvA pAtu prapathe purastAt |yatrAsate sukR^ito yatra te yayustatra tvA devaH savitA dadhAtu || 10.17.4

Apo asmAnmAtaraH shundhayantu ghR^itena no ghR^itapvaH punantu |vishvaM hi ripraM pravahanti devIrudidAbhyaH shuchirA pUta emi || 10.17.10

paraM mR^ityo anu parehi panthAM yaste sva itaro devayAnAt |chakShuShmate shR^iNvate te bravImi mA naH prajAM rIriSho mota vIrAn || 10.18.1

ime jIvA vi mR^itairAvavR^itrannabhUdbhadrA devahUtirno adya |prA~ncho agAma nR^itaye hasAya drAghIya AyuH prataraM dadhAnAH || 10.18.3

ni vartadhvaM mAnu gAtAsmAnsiShakta revatIH |agnIShomA punarvasU asme dhArayataM rayim || 10.19.1

bhadraM no api vAtaya manaH || 10.20.1
agnimILe bhujAM yaviShThaM shAsA mitraM durdharItum |yasya dharmansvarenIH saparyanti mAturUdhaH || 10.20.2

AgniM na svavR^iktibhirhotAraM tvA vR^iNImahe |yaj~nAya stIrNabarhiShe vi vo made shIraM pAvakashochiShaM vivakShase || 10.21.1

kuha shruta indraH kasminnadya jane mitro na shrUyate |R^iShINAM vA yaH kShaye guhA vA charkR^iShe girA || 10.22.1
iha shruta indro asme adya stave vajryR^ichIShamaH |mitro na yo janeShvA yashashchakre asAmyA || 10.22.2

yajAmaha indraM vajradakShiNaM harINAM rathyaM vivratAnAm |pra shmashru dodhuvadUrdhvathA bhUdvi senAbhirdayamAno vi rAdhasA || 10.23.1

so chinnu vR^iShTiryUthyA svA sachA.N indraH shmashrUNi haritAbhi pruShNute |ava veti sukShayaM sute madhUdiddhUnoti vAto yathA vanam || 10.23.4

indra somamimaM piba madhumantaM chamU sutam |asme rayiM ni dhAraya vi vo made sahasriNaM purUvaso vivakShase || 10.24.1

bhadraM no api vAtaya mano dakShamuta kratum |adhA te sakhye andhaso vi vo made raNangAvo na yavase vivakShase || 10.25.1

pra hyachChA manIShA spArhA yanti niyutaH |pra dasrA niyudrathaH pUShA aviShTu mAhinaH || 10.26.1

asatsu me jaritaH sAbhivego yatsunvate yajamAnAya shikSham |anAshIrdAmahamasmi prahantA satyadhvR^itaM vR^ijinAyantamAbhum || 10.27.1
