kiyatI yoShA maryato vadhUyoH pariprItA panyasA vAryeNa |bhadrA vadhUrbhavati yatsupeshAH svayaM sA mitraM vanute jane chit || 10.27.12
patto jagAra pratya~nchamatti shIrShNA shiraH prati dadhau varUtham |AsIna UrdhvAmupasi kShiNAti nya~N~NuttAnAmanveti bhUmim || 10.27.13
bR^ihannachChAyo apalAsho arvA tasthau mAtA viShito atti garbhaH |anyasyA vatsaM rihatI mimAya kayA bhuvA ni dadhe dhenurUdhaH || 10.27.14
sapta vIrAso adharAdudAyannaShTottarAttAtsamajagmirante |nava pashchAtAtsthivimanta Ayandasha prAksAnu vi tirantyashnaH || 10.27.15
dashAnAmekaM kapilaM samAnaM taM hinvanti kratave pAryAya |garbhaM mAtA sudhitaM vakShaNAsvavenantaM tuShayantI bibharti || 10.27.16
pIvAnaM meShamapachanta vIrA nyuptA akShA anu dIva Asan |dvA dhanuM bR^ihatImapsvantaH pavitravantA charataH punantA || 10.27.17
vi kroshanAso viShva~ncha AyanpachAti nemo nahi pakShadardhaH |ayaM me devaH savitA tadAha drvanna idvanavatsarpirannaH || 10.27.18
apashyaM grAmaM vahamAnamArAdachakrayA svadhayA vartamAnam |siShaktyaryaH pra yugA janAnAM sadyaH shishnA praminAno navIyAn || 10.27.19
etau me gAvau pramarasya yuktau mo Shu pra sedhIrmuhurinmamandhi |Apashchidasya vi nashantyarthaM sUrashcha marka uparo babhUvAn || 10.27.20
ayaM yo vajraH purudhA vivR^itto.avaH sUryasya bR^ihataH purIShAt |shrava idenA paro anyadasti tadavyathI jarimANastaranti || 10.27.21
vR^ikShevR^ikShe niyatA mImayadgaustato vayaH pra patAnpUruShAdaH |athedaM vishvaM bhuvanaM bhayAta indrAya sunvadR^iShaye cha shikShat || 10.27.22
devAnAM mAne prathamA atiShThankR^intatrAdeShAmuparA udAyan |trayastapanti pR^ithivImanUpA dvA bR^ibUkaM vahataH purISham || 10.27.23
sA te jIvAturuta tasya viddhi mA smaitAdR^igapa gUhaH samarye |AviH svaH kR^iNute gUhate busaM sa pAdurasya nirNijo na muchyate || 10.27.24

vishvo hyanyo arirAjagAma mamedaha shvashuro nA jagAma |jakShIyAddhAnA uta somaM papIyAtsvAshitaH punarastaM jagAyAt || 10.28.1
sa roruvadvR^iShabhastigmashR^i~Ngo varShmantasthau varimannA pR^ithivyAH |vishveShvenaM vR^ijaneShu pAmi yo me kukShI sutasomaH pR^iNAti || 10.28.2
adriNA te mandina indra tUyAnsunvanti somAnpibasi tvameShAm |pachanti te vR^iShabhA.N atsi teShAM pR^ikSheNa yanmaghavanhUyamAnaH || 10.28.3
idaM su me jaritarA chikiddhi pratIpaM shApaM nadyo vahanti |lopAshaH siMhaM pratya~nchamatsAH kroShTA varAhaM niratakta kakShAt || 10.28.4
kathA ta etadahamA chiketaM gR^itsasya pAkastavaso manIShAm |tvaM no vidvA.N R^ituthA vi vocho yamardhaM te maghavankShemyA dhUH || 10.28.5
evA hi mAM tavasaM vardhayanti divashchinme bR^ihata uttarA dhUH |purU sahasrA ni shishAmi sAkamashatruM hi mA janitA jajAna || 10.28.6
evA hi mAM tavasaM jaj~nurugraM karmankarmanvR^iShaNamindra devAH |vadhIM vR^itraM vajreNa mandasAno.apa vrajaM mahinA dAshuShe vam || 10.28.7
devAsa AyanparashU.NrabibhranvanA vR^ishchanto abhi viDbhirAyan |ni sudrvaM dadhato vakShaNAsu yatrA kR^ipITamanu taddahanti || 10.28.8
shashaH kShuraM pratya~nchaM jagArAdriM logena vyabhedamArAt |bR^ihantaM chidR^ihate randhayAni vayadvatso vR^iShabhaM shUshuvAnaH || 10.28.9
suparNa itthA nakhamA siShAyAvaruddhaH paripadaM na siMhaH |niruddhashchinmahiShastarShyAvAngodhA tasmA ayathaM karShadetat || 10.28.10
tebhyo godhA ayathaM karShadetadye brahmaNaH pratipIyantyannaiH |sima ukShNo.avasR^iShTA.N adanti svayaM balAni tanvaH shR^iNAnAH || 10.28.11
ete shamIbhiH sushamI abhUvanye hinvire tanvaH soma ukthaiH |nR^ivadvadannupa no mAhi vAjAndivi shravo dadhiShe nAma vIraH || 10.28.12

vane na vA yo nyadhAyi chAka~nChuchirvAM stomo bhuraNAvajIgaH |yasyedindraH purudineShu hotA nR^iNAM naryo nR^itamaH kShapAvAn || 10.29.1
pra te asyA uShasaH prAparasyA nR^itau syAma nR^itamasya nR^iNAm |anu trishokaH shatamAvahannR^Inkutsena ratho yo asatsasavAn || 10.29.2
kaste mada indra rantyo bhUdduro giro abhyugro vi dhAva |kadvAho arvAgupa mA manIShA A tvA shakyAmupamaM rAdho annaiH || 10.29.3
kadu dyumnamindra tvAvato nR^InkayA dhiyA karase kanna Agan |mitro na satya urugAya bhR^ityA anne samasya yadasanmanIShAH || 10.29.4
preraya sUro arthaM na pAraM ye asya kAmaM janidhA iva gman |girashcha ye te tuvijAta pUrvIrnara indra pratishikShantyannaiH || 10.29.5
mAtre nu te sumite indra pUrvI dyaurmajmanA pR^ithivI kAvyena |varAya te ghR^itavantaH sutAsaH svAdmanbhavantu pItaye madhUni || 10.29.6
A madhvo asmA asichannamatramindrAya pUrNaM sa hi satyarAdhAH |sa vAvR^idhe varimannA pR^ithivyA abhi kratvA naryaH pauMsyaishcha || 10.29.7
vyAnaLindraH pR^itanAH svojA Asmai yatante sakhyAya pUrvIH |A smA rathaM na pR^itanAsu tiShTha yaM bhadrayA sumatyA chodayAse || 10.29.8

pra devatrA brahmaNe gAturetvapo achChA manaso na prayukti |mahIM mitrasya varuNasya dhAsiM pR^ithujrayase rIradhA suvR^iktim || 10.30.1
adhvaryavo haviShmanto hi bhUtAchChApa itoshatIrushantaH |ava yAshchaShTe aruNaH suparNastamAsyadhvamUrmimadyA suhastAH || 10.30.2
adhvaryavo.apa itA samudramapAM napAtaM haviShA yajadhvam |sa vo dadadUrmimadyA supUtaM tasmai somaM madhumantaM sunota || 10.30.3
yo anidhmo dIdayadapsvantaryaM viprAsa ILate adhvareShu |apAM napAnmadhumatIrapo dA yAbhirindro vAvR^idhe vIryAya || 10.30.4
yAbhiH somo modate harShate cha kalyANIbhiryuvatibhirna maryaH |tA adhvaryo apo achChA parehi yadAsi~nchA oShadhIbhiH punItAt || 10.30.5
evedyUne yuvatayo namanta yadImushannushatIretyachCha |saM jAnate manasA saM chikitre.adhvaryavo dhiShaNApashcha devIH || 10.30.6
yo vo vR^itAbhyo akR^iNodu lokaM yo vo mahyA abhishasteramu~nchat |tasmA indrAya madhumantamUrmiM devamAdanaM pra hiNotanApaH || 10.30.7
prAsmai hinota madhumantamUrmiM garbho yo vaH sindhavo madhva utsaH |ghR^itapR^iShThamIDyamadhvareShvApo revatIH shR^iNutA havaM me || 10.30.8
taM sindhavo matsaramindrapAnamUrmiM pra heta ya ubhe iyarti |madachyutamaushAnaM nabhojAM pari tritantuM vicharantamutsam || 10.30.9
AvarvR^itatIradha nu dvidhArA goShuyudho na niyavaM charantIH |R^iShe janitrIrbhuvanasya patnIrapo vandasva savR^idhaH sayonIH || 10.30.10
hinotA no adhvaraM devayajyA hinota brahma sanaye dhanAnAm |R^itasya yoge vi ShyadhvamUdhaH shruShTIvarIrbhUtanAsmabhyamApaH || 10.30.11
Apo revatIH kShayathA hi vasvaH kratuM cha bhadraM bibhR^ithAmR^itaM cha |rAyashcha stha svapatyasya patnIH sarasvatI tadgR^iNate vayo dhAt || 10.30.12
prati yadApo adR^ishramAyatIrghR^itaM payAMsi bibhratIrmadhUni |adhvaryubhirmanasA saMvidAnA indrAya somaM suShutaM bharantIH || 10.30.13
emA agmanrevatIrjIvadhanyA adhvaryavaH sAdayatA sakhAyaH |ni barhiShi dhattana somyAso.apAM naptrA saMvidAnAsa enAH || 10.30.14
AgmannApa ushatIrbarhiredaM nyadhvare asadandevayantIH |adhvaryavaH sunutendrAya somamabhUdu vaH sushakA devayajyA || 10.30.15

A no devAnAmupa vetu shaMso vishvebhisturairavase yajatraH |tebhirvayaM suShakhAyo bhavema taranto vishvA duritA syAma || 10.31.1
pari chinmarto draviNaM mamanyAdR^itasya pathA namasA vivAset |uta svena kratunA saM vadeta shreyAMsaM dakShaM manasA jagR^ibhyAt || 10.31.2
adhAyi dhItirasasR^igramaMshAstIrthe na dasmamupa yantyUmAH |abhyAnashma suvitasya shUShaM navedaso amR^itAnAmabhUma || 10.31.3
nityashchAkanyAtsvapatirdamUnA yasmA u devaH savitA jajAna |bhago vA gobhiraryamemanajyAtso asmai chArushChadayaduta syAt || 10.31.4
iyaM sA bhUyA uShasAmiva kShA yaddha kShumantaH shavasA samAyan |asya stutiM jariturbhikShamANA A naH shagmAsa upa yantu vAjAH || 10.31.5
asyedeShA sumatiH paprathAnAbhavatpUrvyA bhUmanA gauH |asya sanILA asurasya yonau samAna A bharaNe bibhramANAH || 10.31.6
kiM svidvanaM ka u sa vR^ikSha Asa yato dyAvApR^ithivI niShTatakShuH |saMtasthAne ajare ita/UtI ahAni pUrvIruShaso jaranta || 10.31.7
naitAvadenA paro anyadastyukShA sa dyAvApR^ithivI bibharti |tvachaM pavitraM kR^iNuta svadhAvAnyadIM sUryaM na harito vahanti || 10.31.8
stego na kShAmatyeti pR^ithvIM mihaM na vAto vi ha vAti bhUma |mitro yatra varuNo ajyamAno.agnirvane na vyasR^iShTa shokam || 10.31.9
starIryatsUta sadyo ajyamAnA vyathiravyathIH kR^iNuta svagopA |putro yatpUrvaH pitrorjaniShTa shamyAM gaurjagAra yaddha pR^ichChAn || 10.31.10
uta kaNvaM nR^iShadaH putramAhuruta shyAvo dhanamAdatta vAjI |pra kR^iShNAya rushadapinvatodharR^itamatra nakirasmA apIpet || 10.31.11

pra su gmantA dhiyasAnasya sakShaNi varebhirvarA.N abhi Shu prasIdataH |asmAkamindra ubhayaM jujoShati yatsomyasyAndhaso bubodhati || 10.32.1
vIndra yAsi divyAni rochanA vi pArthivAni rajasA puruShTuta |ye tvA vahanti muhuradhvarA.N upa te su vanvantu vagvanA.N arAdhasaH || 10.32.2
tadinme ChantsadvapuSho vapuShTaraM putro yajjAnaM pitroradhIyati |jAyA patiM vahati vagnunA sumatpuMsa idbhadro vahatuH pariShkR^itaH || 10.32.3
taditsadhasthamabhi chAru dIdhaya gAvo yachChAsanvahatuM na dhenavaH |mAtA yanmanturyUthasya pUrvyAbhi vANasya saptadhAturijjanaH || 10.32.4
pra vo.achChA ririche devayuShpadameko rudrebhiryAti turvaNiH |jarA vA yeShvamR^iteShu dAvane pari va UmebhyaH si~nchatA madhu || 10.32.5
nidhIyamAnamapagULhamapsu pra me devAnAM vratapA uvAcha |indro vidvA.N anu hi tvA chachakSha tenAhamagne anushiShTa AgAm || 10.32.6
akShetravitkShetravidaM hyaprAT sa praiti kShetravidAnushiShTaH |etadvai bhadramanushAsanasyota srutiM vindatya~njasInAm || 10.32.7
adyedu prANIdamamannimAhApIvR^ito adhayanmAturUdhaH |emenamApa jarimA yuvAnamaheLanvasuH sumanA babhUva || 10.32.8
etAni bhadrA kalasha kriyAma kurushravaNa dadato maghAni |dAna idvo maghavAnaH so astvayaM cha somo hR^idi yaM bibharmi || 10.32.9

pra mA yuyujre prayujo janAnAM vahAmi sma pUShaNamantareNa |vishve devAso adha mAmarakShanduHshAsurAgAditi ghoSha AsIt || 10.33.1
saM mA tapantyabhitaH sapatnIriva parshavaH |ni bAdhate amatirnagnatA jasurverna vevIyate matiH || 10.33.2
mUSho na shishnA vyadanti mAdhyaH stotAraM te shatakrato |sakR^itsu no maghavannindra mR^iLayAdhA piteva no bhava || 10.33.3
kurushravaNamAvR^iNi rAjAnaM trAsadasyavam |maMhiShThaM vAghatAmR^iShiH || 10.33.4
yasya mA harito rathe tisro vahanti sAdhuyA |stavai sahasradakShiNe || 10.33.5
yasya prasvAdaso gira upamashravasaH pituH |kShetraM na raNvamUchuShe || 10.33.6
adhi putropamashravo napAnmitrAtitherihi |pituShTe asmi vanditA || 10.33.7
yadIshIyAmR^itAnAmuta vA martyAnAm |jIvedinmaghavA mama || 10.33.8
na devAnAmati vrataM shatAtmA chana jIvati |tathA yujA vi vAvR^ite || 10.33.9

prAvepA mA bR^ihato mAdayanti pravAtejA iriNe varvR^itAnAH |somasyeva maujavatasya bhakSho vibhIdako jAgR^ivirmahyamachChAn || 10.34.1
na mA mimetha na jihILa eShA shivA sakhibhya uta mahyamAsIt |akShasyAhamekaparasya hetoranuvratAmapa jAyAmarodham || 10.34.2
dveShTi shvashrUrapa jAyA ruNaddhi na nAthito vindate marDitAram |ashvasyeva jarato vasnyasya nAhaM vindAmi kitavasya bhogam || 10.34.3
anye jAyAM pari mR^ishantyasya yasyAgR^idhadvedane vAjyakShaH |pitA mAtA bhrAtara enamAhurna jAnImo nayatA baddhametam || 10.34.4
yadAdIdhye na daviShANyebhiH parAyadbhyo.ava hIye sakhibhyaH |nyuptAshcha babhravo vAchamakrata.N emIdeShAM niShkR^itaM jAriNIva || 10.34.5
sabhAmeti kitavaH pR^ichChamAno jeShyAmIti tanvA shUshujAnaH |akShAso asya vi tiranti kAmaM pratidIvne dadhata A kR^itAni || 10.34.6
akShAsa ida~Nkushino nitodino nikR^itvAnastapanAstApayiShNavaH |kumAradeShNA jayataH punarhaNo madhvA sampR^iktAH kitavasya barhaNA || 10.34.7
tripa~nchAshaH krILati vrAta eShAM deva iva savitA satyadharmA |ugrasya chinmanyave nA namante rAjA chidebhyo nama itkR^iNoti || 10.34.8
nIchA vartanta upari sphurantyahastAso hastavantaM sahante |divyA a~NgArA iriNe nyuptAH shItAH santo hR^idayaM nirdahanti || 10.34.9
jAyA tapyate kitavasya hInA mAtA putrasya charataH kva svit |R^iNAvA bibhyaddhanamichChamAno.anyeShAmastamupa naktameti || 10.34.10
striyaM dR^iShTvAya kitavaM tatApAnyeShAM jAyAM sukR^itaM cha yonim |pUrvAhNe ashvAnyuyuje hi babhrUnso agnerante vR^iShalaH papAda || 10.34.11
yo vaH senAnIrmahato gaNasya rAjA vrAtasya prathamo babhUva |tasmai kR^iNomi na dhanA ruNadhmi dashAhaM prAchIstadR^itaM vadAmi || 10.34.12
akShairmA dIvyaH kR^iShimitkR^iShasva vitte ramasva bahu manyamAnaH |tatra gAvaH kitava tatra jAyA tanme vi chaShTe savitAyamaryaH || 10.34.13
mitraM kR^iNudhvaM khalu mR^iLatA no mA no ghoreNa charatAbhi dhR^iShNu |ni vo nu manyurvishatAmarAtiranyo babhrUNAM prasitau nvastu || 10.34.14

abudhramu tya indravanto agnayo jyotirbharanta uShaso vyuShTiShu |mahI dyAvApR^ithivI chetatAmapo.adyA devAnAmava A vR^iNImahe || 10.35.1
divaspR^ithivyorava A vR^iNImahe mAtR^InsindhUnparvatA~nCharyaNAvataH |anAgAstvaM sUryamuShAsamImahe bhadraM somaH suvAno adyA kR^iNotu naH || 10.35.2
dyAvA no adya pR^ithivI anAgaso mahI trAyetAM suvitAya mAtarA |uShA uchChantyapa bAdhatAmaghaM svastyagniM samidhAnamImahe || 10.35.3
iyaM na usrA prathamA sudevyaM revatsanibhyo revatI vyuchChatu |Are manyuM durvidatrasya dhImahi svastyagniM samidhAnamImahe || 10.35.4
pra yAH sisrate sUryasya rashmibhirjyotirbharantIruShaso vyuShTiShu |bhadrA no adya shravase vyuchChata svastyagniM samidhAnamImahe || 10.35.5
anamIvA uShasa A charantu na udagnayo jihatAM jyotiShA bR^ihat |AyukShAtAmashvinA tUtujiM rathaM svastyagniM samidhAnamImahe || 10.35.6
shreShThaM no adya savitarvareNyaM bhAgamA suva sa hi ratnadhA asi |rAyo janitrIM dhiShaNAmupa bruve svastyagniM samidhAnamImahe || 10.35.7
pipartu mA tadR^itasya pravAchanaM devAnAM yanmanuShyA amanmahi |vishvA idusrAH spaLudeti sUryaH svastyagniM samidhAnamImahe || 10.35.8
adveSho adya barhiShaH starImaNi grAvNAM yoge manmanaH sAdha Imahe |AdityAnAM sharmaNi sthA bhuraNyasi svastyagniM samidhAnamImahe || 10.35.9
A no barhiH sadhamAde bR^ihaddivi devA.N ILe sAdayA sapta hotR^In |indraM mitraM varuNaM sAtaye bhagaM svastyagniM samidhAnamImahe || 10.35.10
ta AdityA A gatA sarvatAtaye vR^idhe no yaj~namavatA sajoShasaH |bR^ihaspatiM pUShaNamashvinA bhagaM svastyagniM samidhAnamImahe || 10.35.11
tanno devA yachChata supravAchanaM ChardirAdityAH subharaM nR^ipAyyam |pashve tokAya tanayAya jIvase svastyagniM samidhAnamImahe || 10.35.12
vishve adya maruto vishva UtI vishve bhavantvagnayaH samiddhAH |vishve no devA avasA gamantu vishvamastu draviNaM vAjo asme || 10.35.13
yaM devAso.avatha vAjasAtau yaM trAyadhve yaM pipR^ithAtyaMhaH |yo vo gopIthe na bhayasya veda te syAma devavItaye turAsaH || 10.35.14

uShAsAnaktA bR^ihatI supeshasA dyAvAkShAmA varuNo mitro aryamA |indraM huve marutaH parvatA.N apa AdityAndyAvApR^ithivI apaH svaH || 10.36.1
dyaushcha naH pR^ithivI cha prachetasa R^itAvarI rakShatAmaMhaso riShaH |mA durvidatrA nirR^itirna Ishata taddevAnAmavo adyA vR^iNImahe || 10.36.2
vishvasmAnno aditiH pAtvaMhaso mAtA mitrasya varuNasya revataH |svarvajjyotiravR^ikaM nashImahi taddevAnAmavo adyA vR^iNImahe || 10.36.3
grAvA vadannapa rakShAMsi sedhatu duShShvapnyaM nirR^itiM vishvamatriNam |AdityaM sharma marutAmashImahi taddevAnAmavo adyA vR^iNImahe || 10.36.4
endro barhiH sIdatu pinvatAmiLA bR^ihaspatiH sAmabhirR^ikvo archatu |supraketaM jIvase manma dhImahi taddevAnAmavo adyA vR^iNImahe || 10.36.5
divispR^ishaM yaj~namasmAkamashvinA jIrAdhvaraM kR^iNutaM sumnamiShTaye |prAchInarashmimAhutaM ghR^itena taddevAnAmavo adyA vR^iNImahe || 10.36.6
upa hvaye suhavaM mArutaM gaNaM pAvakamR^iShvaM sakhyAya shambhuvam |rAyaspoShaM saushravasAya dhImahi taddevAnAmavo adyA vR^iNImahe || 10.36.7
apAM peruM jIvadhanyaM bharAmahe devAvyaM suhavamadhvarashriyam |surashmiM somamindriyaM yamImahi taddevAnAmavo adyA vR^iNImahe || 10.36.8
sanema tatsusanitA sanitvabhirvayaM jIvA jIvaputrA anAgasaH |brahmadviSho viShvageno bharerata taddevAnAmavo adyA vR^iNImahe || 10.36.9
ye sthA manoryaj~niyAste shR^iNotana yadvo devA Imahe taddadAtana |jaitraM kratuM rayimadvIravadyashastaddevAnAmavo adyA vR^iNImahe || 10.36.10
mahadadya mahatAmA vR^iNImahe.avo devAnAM bR^ihatAmanarvaNAm |yathA vasu vIrajAtaM nashAmahai taddevAnAmavo adyA vR^iNImahe || 10.36.11
maho agneH samidhAnasya sharmaNyanAgA mitre varuNe svastaye |shreShThe syAma savituH savImani taddevAnAmavo adyA vR^iNImahe || 10.36.12
ye savituH satyasavasya vishve mitrasya vrate varuNasya devAH |te saubhagaM vIravadgomadapno dadhAtana draviNaM chitramasme || 10.36.13
savitA pashchAtAtsavitA purastAtsavitottarAttAtsavitAdharAttAt |savitA naH suvatu sarvatAtiM savitA no rAsatAM dIrghamAyuH || 10.36.14

namo mitrasya varuNasya chakShase maho devAya tadR^itaM saparyata |dUredR^ishe devajAtAya ketave divasputrAya sUryAya shaMsata || 10.37.1
sA mA satyoktiH pari pAtu vishvato dyAvA cha yatra tatanannahAni cha |vishvamanyanni vishate yadejati vishvAhApo vishvAhodeti sUryaH || 10.37.2
na te adevaH pradivo ni vAsate yadetashebhiH patarai ratharyasi |prAchInamanyadanu vartate raja udanyena jyotiShA yAsi sUrya || 10.37.3
yena sUrya jyotiShA bAdhase tamo jagachcha vishvamudiyarShi bhAnunA |tenAsmadvishvAmanirAmanAhutimapAmIvAmapa duShShvapnyaM suva || 10.37.4
vishvasya hi preShito rakShasi vratamaheLayannuchcharasi svadhA anu |yadadya tvA sUryopabravAmahai taM no devA anu maMsIrata kratum || 10.37.5
taM no dyAvApR^ithivI tanna Apa indraH shR^iNvantu maruto havaM vachaH |mA shUne bhUma sUryasya saMdR^ishi bhadraM jIvanto jaraNAmashImahi || 10.37.6
vishvAhA tvA sumanasaH suchakShasaH prajAvanto anamIvA anAgasaH |udyantaM tvA mitramaho divedive jyogjIvAH prati pashyema sUrya || 10.37.7
mahi jyotirbibhrataM tvA vichakShaNa bhAsvantaM chakShuShechakShuShe mayaH |ArohantaM bR^ihataH pAjasaspari vayaM jIvAH prati pashyema sUrya || 10.37.8
yasya te vishvA bhuvanAni ketunA pra cherate ni cha vishante aktubhiH |anAgAstvena harikesha sUryAhnAhnA no vasyasAvasyasodihi || 10.37.9
shaM no bhava chakShasA shaM no ahnA shaM bhAnunA shaM himA shaM ghR^iNena |yathA shamadhva~nChamasadduroNe tatsUrya draviNaM dhehi chitram || 10.37.10
asmAkaM devA ubhayAya janmane sharma yachChata dvipade chatuShpade |adatpibadUrjayamAnamAshitaM tadasme shaM yorarapo dadhAtana || 10.37.11
yadvo devAshchakR^ima jihvayA guru manaso vA prayutI devaheLanam |arAvA yo no abhi duchChunAyate tasmintadeno vasavo ni dhetana || 10.37.12

asminna indra pR^itsutau yashasvati shimIvati krandasi prAva sAtaye |yatra goShAtA dhR^iShiteShu khAdiShu viShvakpatanti didyavo nR^iShAhye || 10.38.1
sa naH kShumantaM sadane vyUrNuhi go/arNasaM rayimindra shravAyyam |syAma te jayataH shakra medino yathA vayamushmasi tadvaso kR^idhi || 10.38.2
yo no dAsa Aryo vA puruShTutAdeva indra yudhaye chiketati |asmAbhiShTe suShahAH santu shatravastvayA vayaM tAnvanuyAma saMgame || 10.38.3
yo dabhrebhirhavyo yashcha bhUribhiryo abhIke varivovinnR^iShAhye |taM vikhAde sasnimadya shrutaM naramarvA~nchamindramavase karAmahe || 10.38.4
svavR^ijaM hi tvAmahamindra shushravAnAnudaM vR^iShabha radhrachodanam |pra mu~nchasva pari kutsAdihA gahi kimu tvAvAnmuShkayorbaddha Asate || 10.38.5

yo vAM parijmA suvR^idashvinA ratho doShAmuShAso havyo haviShmatA |shashvattamAsastamu vAmidaM vayaM piturna nAma suhavaM havAmahe || 10.39.1
chodayataM sUnR^itAH pinvataM dhiya utpuraMdhIrIrayataM tadushmasi |yashasaM bhAgaM kR^iNutaM no ashvinA somaM na chAruM maghavatsu naskR^itam || 10.39.2
amAjurashchidbhavatho yuvaM bhago.anAshoshchidavitArApamasya chit |andhasya chinnAsatyA kR^ishasya chidyuvAmidAhurbhiShajA rutasya chit || 10.39.3
yuvaM chyavAnaM sanayaM yathA rathaM punaryuvAnaM charathAya takShathuH |niShTaugryamUhathuradbhyaspari vishvettA vAM savaneShu pravAchyA || 10.39.4
purANA vAM vIryA pra bravA jane.atho hAsathurbhiShajA mayobhuvA |tA vAM nu navyAvavase karAmahe.ayaM nAsatyA shradariryathA dadhat || 10.39.5
iyaM vAmahve shR^iNutaM me ashvinA putrAyeva pitarA mahyaM shikShatam |anApiraj~nA asajAtyAmatiH purA tasyA abhishasterava spR^itam || 10.39.6
yuvaM rathena vimadAya shundhyuvaM nyUhathuH purumitrasya yoShaNAm |yuvaM havaM vadhrimatyA agachChataM yuvaM suShutiM chakrathuH puraMdhaye || 10.39.7
yuvaM viprasya jaraNAmupeyuShaH punaH kalerakR^iNutaM yuvadvayaH |yuvaM vandanamR^ishyadAdudUpathuryuvaM sadyo vishpalAmetave kR^ithaH || 10.39.8
yuvaM ha rebhaM vR^iShaNA guhA hitamudairayataM mamR^ivAMsamashvinA |yuvamR^ibIsamuta taptamatraya omanvantaM chakrathuH saptavadhraye || 10.39.9
yuvaM shvetaM pedave.ashvinAshvaM navabhirvAjairnavatI cha vAjinam |charkR^ityaM dadathurdrAvayatsakhaM bhagaM na nR^ibhyo havyaM mayobhuvam || 10.39.10
na taM rAjAnAvadite kutashchana nAMho ashnoti duritaM nakirbhayam |yamashvinA suhavA rudravartanI purorathaM kR^iNuthaH patnyA saha || 10.39.11
A tena yAtaM manaso javIyasA rathaM yaM vAmR^ibhavashchakrurashvinA |yasya yoge duhitA jAyate diva ubhe ahanI sudine vivasvataH || 10.39.12
tA vartiryAtaM jayuShA vi parvatamapinvataM shayave dhenumashvinA |vR^ikasya chidvartikAmantarAsyAdyuvaM shachIbhirgrasitAmamu~nchatam || 10.39.13
etaM vAM stomamashvinAvakarmAtakShAma bhR^igavo na ratham |nyamR^ikShAma yoShaNAM na marye nityaM na sUnuM tanayaM dadhAnAH || 10.39.14

rathaM yAntaM kuha ko ha vAM narA prati dyumantaM suvitAya bhUShati |prAtaryAvANaM vibhvaM vishevishe vastorvastorvahamAnaM dhiyA shami || 10.40.1
kuha sviddoShA kuha vastorashvinA kuhAbhipitvaM karataH kuhoShatuH |ko vAM shayutrA vidhaveva devaraM maryaM na yoShA kR^iNute sadhastha A || 10.40.2
prAtarjarethe jaraNeva kApayA vastorvastoryajatA gachChatho gR^iham |kasya dhvasrA bhavathaH kasya vA narA rAjaputreva savanAva gachChathaH || 10.40.3
yuvAM mR^igeva vAraNA mR^igaNyavo doShA vastorhaviShA ni hvayAmahe |yuvaM hotrAmR^ituthA juhvate nareShaM janAya vahathaH shubhaspatI || 10.40.4
yuvAM ha ghoShA paryashvinA yatI rAj~na Uche duhitA pR^ichChe vAM narA |bhUtaM me ahna uta bhUtamaktave.ashvAvate rathine shaktamarvate || 10.40.5
yuvaM kavI ShThaH paryashvinA rathaM visho na kutso jariturnashAyathaH |yuvorha makShA paryashvinA madhvAsA bharata niShkR^itaM na yoShaNA || 10.40.6
yuvaM ha bhujyuM yuvamashvinA vashaM yuvaM shi~njAramushanAmupArathuH |yuvo rarAvA pari sakhyamAsate yuvorahamavasA sumnamA chake || 10.40.7
yuvaM ha kR^ishaM yuvamashvinA shayuM yuvaM vidhantaM vidhavAmuruShyathaH |yuvaM sanibhyaH stanayantamashvinApa vrajamUrNuthaH saptAsyam || 10.40.8
janiShTa yoShA patayatkanInako vi chAruhanvIrudho daMsanA anu |Asmai rIyante nivaneva sindhavo.asmA ahne bhavati tatpatitvanam || 10.40.9
jIvaM rudanti vi mayante adhvare dIrghAmanu prasitiM dIdhiyurnaraH |vAmaM pitR^ibhyo ya idaM samerire mayaH patibhyo janayaH pariShvaje || 10.40.10
na tasya vidma tadu Shu pra vochata yuvA ha yadyuvatyAH kSheti yoniShu |priyosriyasya vR^iShabhasya retino gR^ihaM gamemAshvinA tadushmasi || 10.40.11
A vAmagansumatirvAjinIvasU nyashvinA hR^itsu kAmA ayaMsata |abhUtaM gopA mithunA shubhaspatI priyA aryamNo duryA.N ashImahi || 10.40.12
tA mandasAnA manuSho duroNa A dhattaM rayiM sahavIraM vachasyave |kR^itaM tIrthaM suprapANaM shubhaspatI sthANuM patheShThAmapa durmatiM hatam || 10.40.13
kva svidadya katamAsvashvinA vikShu dasrA mAdayete shubhaspatI |ka IM ni yeme katamasya jagmaturviprasya vA yajamAnasya vA gR^iham || 10.40.14

samAnamu tyaM puruhUtamukthyaM rathaM trichakraM savanA ganigmatam |parijmAnaM vidathyaM suvR^iktibhirvayaM vyuShTA uShaso havAmahe || 10.41.1
prAtaryujaM nAsatyAdhi tiShThathaH prAtaryAvANaM madhuvAhanaM ratham |visho yena gachChatho yajvarIrnarA kIreshchidyaj~naM hotR^imantamashvinA || 10.41.2
adhvaryuM vA madhupANiM suhastyamagnidhaM vA dhR^itadakShaM damUnasam |viprasya vA yatsavanAni gachChatho.ata A yAtaM madhupeyamashvinA || 10.41.3

asteva su prataraM lAyamasyanbhUShanniva pra bharA stomamasmai |vAchA viprAstarata vAchamaryo ni rAmaya jaritaH soma indram || 10.42.1
dohena gAmupa shikShA sakhAyaM pra bodhaya jaritarjAramindram |koshaM na pUrNaM vasunA nyR^iShTamA chyAvaya maghadeyAya shUram || 10.42.2
kima~Nga tvA maghavanbhojamAhuH shishIhi mA shishayaM tvA shR^iNomi |apnasvatI mama dhIrastu shakra vasuvidaM bhagamindrA bharA naH || 10.42.3
tvAM janA mamasatyeShvindra saMtasthAnA vi hvayante samIke |atrA yujaM kR^iNute yo haviShmAnnAsunvatA sakhyaM vaShTi shUraH || 10.42.4
dhanaM na syandraM bahulaM yo asmai tIvrAnsomA.N Asunoti prayasvAn |tasmai shatrUnsutukAnprAtarahno ni svaShTrAnyuvati hanti vR^itram || 10.42.5
yasminvayaM dadhimA shaMsamindre yaH shishrAya maghavA kAmamasme |ArAchchitsanbhayatAmasya shatrurnyasmai dyumnA janyA namantAm || 10.42.6
ArAchChatrumapa bAdhasva dUramugro yaH shambaH puruhUta tena |asme dhehi yavamadgomadindra kR^idhI dhiyaM jaritre vAjaratnAm || 10.42.7
pra yamantarvR^iShasavAso agmantIvrAH somA bahulAntAsa indram |nAha dAmAnaM maghavA ni yaMsanni sunvate vahati bhUri vAmam || 10.42.8
uta prahAmatidIvyA jayAti kR^itaM yachChvaghnI vichinoti kAle |yo devakAmo na dhanA ruNaddhi samittaM rAyA sR^ijati svadhAvAn || 10.42.9
gobhiShTaremAmatiM durevAM yavena kShudhaM puruhUta vishvAm |vayaM rAjabhiH prathamA dhanAnyasmAkena vR^ijanenA jayema || 10.42.10
bR^ihaspatirnaH pari pAtu pashchAdutottarasmAdadharAdaghAyoH |indraH purastAduta madhyato naH sakhA sakhibhyo varivaH kR^iNotu || 10.42.11

achChA ma indraM matayaH svarvidaH sadhrIchIrvishvA ushatIranUShata |pari Shvajante janayo yathA patiM maryaM na shundhyuM maghavAnamUtaye || 10.43.1
na ghA tvadrigapa veti me manastve itkAmaM puruhUta shishraya |rAjeva dasma ni Shado.adhi barhiShyasminsu some.avapAnamastu te || 10.43.2
viShUvR^idindro amateruta kShudhaH sa idrAyo maghavA vasva Ishate |tasyedime pravaNe sapta sindhavo vayo vardhanti vR^iShabhasya shuShmiNaH || 10.43.3
vayo na vR^ikShaM supalAshamAsadansomAsa indraM mandinashchamUShadaH |praiShAmanIkaM shavasA davidyutadvidatsvarmanave jyotirAryam || 10.43.4
kR^itaM na shvaghnI vi chinoti devane saMvargaM yanmaghavA sUryaM jayat |na tatte anyo anu vIryaM shakanna purANo maghavannota nUtanaH || 10.43.5
vishaMvishaM maghavA paryashAyata janAnAM dhenA avachAkashadvR^iShA |yasyAha shakraH savaneShu raNyati sa tIvraiH somaiH sahate pR^itanyataH || 10.43.6
Apo na sindhumabhi yatsamakSharansomAsa indraM kulyA iva hradam |vardhanti viprA maho asya sAdane yavaM na vR^iShTirdivyena dAnunA || 10.43.7
vR^iShA na kruddhaH patayadrajassvA yo aryapatnIrakR^iNodimA apaH |sa sunvate maghavA jIradAnave.avindajjyotirmanave haviShmate || 10.43.8
ujjAyatAM parashurjyotiShA saha bhUyA R^itasya sudughA purANavat |vi rochatAmaruSho bhAnunA shuchiH svarNa shukraM shushuchIta satpatiH || 10.43.9
gobhiShTaremAmatiM durevAM yavena kShudhaM puruhUta vishvAm |vayaM rAjabhiH prathamA dhanAnyasmAkena vR^ijanenA jayema || 10.43.10
bR^ihaspatirnaH pari pAtu pashchAdutottarasmAdadharAdaghAyoH |indraH purastAduta madhyato naH sakhA sakhibhyo varivaH kR^iNotu || 10.43.11

A yAtvindraH svapatirmadAya yo dharmaNA tUtujAnastuviShmAn |pratvakShANo ati vishvA sahAMsyapAreNa mahatA vR^iShNyena || 10.44.1
suShThAmA rathaH suyamA harI te mimyakSha vajro nR^ipate gabhastau |shIbhaM rAjansupathA yAhyarvA~NvardhAma te papuSho vR^iShNyAni || 10.44.2
endravAho nR^ipatiM vajrabAhumugramugrAsastaviShAsa enam |pratvakShasaM vR^iShabhaM satyashuShmamemasmatrA sadhamAdo vahantu || 10.44.3
evA patiM droNasAchaM sachetasamUrjaH skambhaM dharuNa A vR^iShAyase |ojaH kR^iShva saM gR^ibhAya tve apyaso yathA kenipAnAmino vR^idhe || 10.44.4
gamannasme vasUnyA hi shaMsiShaM svAshiShaM bharamA yAhi sominaH |tvamIshiShe sAsminnA satsi barhiShyanAdhR^iShyA tava pAtrANi dharmaNA || 10.44.5
pR^ithakprAyanprathamA devahUtayo.akR^iNvata shravasyAni duShTarA |na ye shekuryaj~niyAM nAvamAruhamIrmaiva te nyavishanta kepayaH || 10.44.6
evaivApAgapare santu dUDhyo.ashvA yeShAM duryuja Ayuyujre |itthA ye prAgupare santi dAvane purUNi yatra vayunAni bhojanA || 10.44.7
girI.NrajrAnrejamAnA.N adhArayaddyauH krandadantarikShANi kopayat |samIchIne dhiShaNe vi ShkabhAyati vR^iShNaH pItvA mada ukthAni shaMsati || 10.44.8
imaM bibharmi sukR^itaM te a~NkushaM yenArujAsi maghava~nChaphArujaH |asminsu te savane astvokyaM suta iShTau maghavanbodhyAbhagaH || 10.44.9
gobhiShTaremAmatiM durevAM yavena kShudhaM puruhUta vishvAm |vayaM rAjabhiH prathamA dhanAnyasmAkena vR^ijanenA jayema || 10.44.10
bR^ihaspatirnaH pari pAtu pashchAdutottarasmAdadharAdaghAyoH |indraH purastAduta madhyato naH sakhA sakhibhyo varivaH kR^iNotu || 10.44.11

divaspari prathamaM jaj~ne agnirasmaddvitIyaM pari jAtavedAH |tR^itIyamapsu nR^imaNA ajasramindhAna enaM jarate svAdhIH || 10.45.1
vidmA te agne tredhA trayANi vidmA te dhAma vibhR^itA purutrA |vidmA te nAma paramaM guhA yadvidmA tamutsaM yata Ajagantha || 10.45.2
samudre tvA nR^imaNA apsvantarnR^ichakShA Idhe divo agna Udhan |tR^itIye tvA rajasi tasthivAMsamapAmupasthe mahiShA avardhan || 10.45.3
akrandadagniH stanayanniva dyauH kShAmA rerihadvIrudhaH sama~njan |sadyo jaj~nAno vi hImiddho akhyadA rodasI bhAnunA bhAtyantaH || 10.45.4
shrINAmudAro dharuNo rayINAM manIShANAM prArpaNaH somagopAH |vasuH sUnuH sahaso apsu rAjA vi bhAtyagra uShasAmidhAnaH || 10.45.5
vishvasya keturbhuvanasya garbha A rodasI apR^iNAjjAyamAnaH |vILuM chidadrimabhinatparAya~njanA yadagnimayajanta pa~ncha || 10.45.6
ushikpAvako aratiH sumedhA marteShvagniramR^ito ni dhAyi |iyarti dhUmamaruShaM bharibhraduchChukreNa shochiShA dyAminakShan || 10.45.7
dR^ishAno rukma urviyA vyadyauddurmarShamAyuH shriye ruchAnaH |agniramR^ito abhavadvayobhiryadenaM dyaurjanayatsuretAH || 10.45.8
yaste adya kR^iNavadbhadrashoche.apUpaM deva ghR^itavantamagne |pra taM naya prataraM vasyo achChAbhi sumnaM devabhaktaM yaviShTha || 10.45.9
A taM bhaja saushravaseShvagna ukthauktha A bhaja shasyamAne |priyaH sUrye priyo agnA bhavAtyujjAtena bhinadadujjanitvaiH || 10.45.10
tvAmagne yajamAnA anu dyUnvishvA vasu dadhire vAryANi |tvayA saha draviNamichChamAnA vrajaM gomantamushijo vi vavruH || 10.45.11
astAvyagnirnarAM sushevo vaishvAnara R^iShibhiH somagopAH |adveShe dyAvApR^ithivI huvema devA dhatta rayimasme suvIram || 10.45.12

pra hotA jAto mahAnnabhovinnR^iShadvA sIdadapAmupasthe |dadhiryo dhAyi sa te vayAMsi yantA vasUni vidhate tanUpAH || 10.46.1
imaM vidhanto apAM sadhasthe pashuM na naShTaM padairanu gman |guhA chatantamushijo namobhirichChanto dhIrA bhR^igavo.avindan || 10.46.2
imaM trito bhUryavindadichChanvaibhUvaso mUrdhanyaghnyAyAH |sa shevR^idho jAta A harmyeShu nAbhiryuvA bhavati rochanasya || 10.46.3
mandraM hotAramushijo namobhiH prA~nchaM yaj~naM netAramadhvarANAm |vishAmakR^iNvannaratiM pAvakaM havyavAhaM dadhato mAnuSheShu || 10.46.4
pra bhUrjayantaM mahAM vipodhAM mUrA amUraM purAM darmANam |nayanto garbhaM vanAM dhiyaM dhurhirishmashruM nArvANaM dhanarcham || 10.46.5
ni pastyAsu tritaH stabhUyanparivIto yonau sIdadantaH |ataH saMgR^ibhyA vishAM damUnA vidharmaNAyantrairIyate nR^In || 10.46.6
asyAjarAso damAmaritrA archaddhUmAso agnayaH pAvakAH |shvitIchayaH shvAtrAso bhuraNyavo vanarShado vAyavo na somAH || 10.46.7
pra jihvayA bharate vepo agniH pra vayunAni chetasA pR^ithivyAH |tamAyavaH shuchayantaM pAvakaM mandraM hotAraM dadhire yajiShTham || 10.46.8
dyAvA yamagniM pR^ithivI janiShTAmApastvaShTA bhR^igavo yaM sahobhiH |ILenyaM prathamaM mAtarishvA devAstatakShurmanave yajatram || 10.46.9
yaM tvA devA dadhire havyavAhaM puruspR^iho mAnuShAso yajatram |sa yAmannagne stuvate vayo dhAH pra devayanyashasaH saM hi pUrvIH || 10.46.10

jagR^ibhmA te dakShiNamindra hastaM vasUyavo vasupate vasUnAm |vidmA hi tvA gopatiM shUra gonAmasmabhyaM chitraM vR^iShaNaM rayiM dAH || 10.47.1
svAyudhaM svavasaM sunIthaM chatuHsamudraM dharuNaM rayINAm |charkR^ityaM shaMsyaM bhUrivAramasmabhyaM chitraM vR^iShaNaM rayiM dAH || 10.47.2
subrahmANaM devavantaM bR^ihantamuruM gabhIraM pR^ithubudhnamindra |shrutaR^iShimugramabhimAtiShAhamasmabhyaM chitraM vR^iShaNaM rayiM dAH || 10.47.3
sanadvAjaM vipravIraM tarutraM dhanaspR^itaM shUshuvAMsaM sudakSham |dasyuhanaM pUrbhidamindra satyamasmabhyaM chitraM vR^iShaNaM rayiM dAH || 10.47.4
ashvAvantaM rathinaM vIravantaM sahasriNaM shatinaM vAjamindra |bhadravrAtaM vipravIraM svarShAmasmabhyaM chitraM vR^iShaNaM rayiM dAH || 10.47.5
pra saptagumR^itadhItiM sumedhAM bR^ihaspatiM matirachChA jigAti |ya A~Ngiraso namasopasadyo.asmabhyaM chitraM vR^iShaNaM rayiM dAH || 10.47.6
vanIvAno mama dUtAsa indraM stomAshcharanti sumatIriyAnAH |hR^idispR^isho manasA vachyamAnA asmabhyaM chitraM vR^iShaNaM rayiM dAH || 10.47.7
yattvA yAmi daddhi tanna indra bR^ihantaM kShayamasamaM janAnAm |abhi taddyAvApR^ithivI gR^iNItAmasmabhyaM chitraM vR^iShaNaM rayiM dAH || 10.47.8

ahaM bhuvaM vasunaH pUrvyaspatirahaM dhanAni saM jayAmi shashvataH |mAM havante pitaraM na jantavo.ahaM dAshuShe vi bhajAmi bhojanam || 10.48.1
ahamindro rodho vakSho atharvaNastritAya gA ajanayamaheradhi |ahaM dasyubhyaH pari nR^imNamA dade gotrA shikShandadhIche mAtarishvane || 10.48.2
mahyaM tvaShTA vajramatakShadAyasaM mayi devAso.avR^ijannapi kratum |mamAnIkaM sUryasyeva duShTaraM mAmAryanti kR^itena kartvena cha || 10.48.3
ahametaM gavyayamashvyaM pashuM purIShiNaM sAyakenA hiraNyayam |purU sahasrA ni shishAmi dAshuShe yanmA somAsa ukthino amandiShuH || 10.48.4
ahamindro na parA jigya iddhanaM na mR^ityave.ava tasthe kadA chana |somaminmA sunvanto yAchatA vasu na me pUravaH sakhye riShAthana || 10.48.5
ahametA~nChAshvasato dvAdvendraM ye vajraM yudhaye.akR^iNvata |AhvayamAnA.N ava hanmanAhanaM dR^iLhA vadannanamasyurnamasvinaH || 10.48.6
abhIdamekameko asmi niShShALabhI dvA kimu trayaH karanti |khale na parShAnprati hanmi bhUri kiM mA nindanti shatravo.anindrAH || 10.48.7
ahaM gu~Ngubhyo atithigvamiShkaramiShaM na vR^itraturaM vikShu dhArayam |yatparNayaghna uta vA kara~njahe prAhaM mahe vR^itrahatye ashushravi || 10.48.8
pra me namI sApya iShe bhuje bhUdgavAmeShe sakhyA kR^iNuta dvitA |didyuM yadasya samitheShu maMhayamAdidenaM shaMsyamukthyaM karam || 10.48.9
pra nemasmindadR^ishe somo antargopA nemamAvirasthA kR^iNoti |sa tigmashR^i~NgaM vR^iShabhaM yuyutsandruhastasthau bahule baddho antaH || 10.48.10
AdityAnAM vasUnAM rudriyANAM devo devAnAM na minAmi dhAma |te mA bhadrAya shavase tatakShuraparAjitamastR^itamaShALham || 10.48.11

ahaM dAM gR^iNate pUrvyaM vasvahaM brahma kR^iNavaM mahyaM vardhanam |ahaM bhuvaM yajamAnasya choditAyajvanaH sAkShi vishvasminbhare || 10.49.1
mAM dhurindraM nAma devatA divashcha gmashchApAM cha jantavaH |ahaM harI vR^iShaNA vivratA raghU ahaM vajraM shavase dhR^iShNvA dade || 10.49.2
ahamatkaM kavaye shishnathaM hathairahaM kutsamAvamAbhirUtibhiH |ahaM shuShNasya shnathitA vadharyamaM na yo rara AryaM nAma dasyave || 10.49.3
ahaM piteva vetasU.NrabhiShTaye tugraM kutsAya smadibhaM cha randhayam |ahaM bhuvaM yajamAnasya rAjani pra yadbhare tujaye na priyAdhR^iShe || 10.49.4
ahaM randhayaM mR^igayaM shrutarvaNe yanmAjihIta vayunA chanAnuShak |ahaM veshaM namramAyave.akaramahaM savyAya paDgR^ibhimarandhayam || 10.49.5
ahaM sa yo navavAstvaM bR^ihadrathaM saM vR^itreva dAsaM vR^itrahArujam |yadvardhayantaM prathayantamAnuShagdUre pAre rajaso rochanAkaram || 10.49.6
ahaM sUryasya pari yAmyAshubhiH praitashebhirvahamAna ojasA |yanmA sAvo manuSha Aha nirNija R^idhakkR^iShe dAsaM kR^itvyaM hathaiH || 10.49.7
ahaM saptahA nahuSho nahuShTaraH prAshrAvayaM shavasA turvashaM yadum |ahaM nyanyaM sahasA sahaskaraM nava vrAdhato navatiM cha vakShayam || 10.49.8
ahaM sapta sravato dhArayaM vR^iShA dravitnvaH pR^ithivyAM sIrA adhi |ahamarNAMsi vi tirAmi sukraturyudhA vidaM manave gAtumiShTaye || 10.49.9
ahaM tadAsu dhArayaM yadAsu na devashchana tvaShTAdhArayadrushat |spArhaM gavAmUdhassu vakShaNAsvA madhormadhu shvAtryaM somamAshiram || 10.49.10
evA devA.N indro vivye nR^Inpra chyautnena maghavA satyarAdhAH |vishvettA te harivaH shachIvo.abhi turAsaH svayasho gR^iNanti || 10.49.11

pra vo mahe mandamAnAyAndhaso.archA vishvAnarAya vishvAbhuve |indrasya yasya sumakhaM saho mahi shravo nR^imNaM cha rodasI saparyataH || 10.50.1
so chinnu sakhyA narya inaH stutashcharkR^itya indro mAvate nare |vishvAsu dhUrShu vAjakR^ityeShu satpate vR^itre vApsvabhi shUra mandase || 10.50.2
ke te nara indra ye ta iShe ye te sumnaM sadhanyamiyakShAn |ke te vAjAyAsuryAya hinvire ke apsu svAsUrvarAsu pauMsye || 10.50.3
bhuvastvamindra brahmaNA mahAnbhuvo vishveShu savaneShu yaj~niyaH |bhuvo nR^I.Nshchyautno vishvasminbhare jyeShThashcha mantro vishvacharShaNe || 10.50.4
avA nu kaM jyAyAnyaj~navanaso mahIM ta omAtrAM kR^iShTayo viduH |aso nu kamajaro vardhAshcha vishvedetA savanA tUtumA kR^iShe || 10.50.5
etA vishvA savanA tUtumA kR^iShe svayaM sUno sahaso yAni dadhiShe |varAya te pAtraM dharmaNe tanA yaj~no mantro brahmodyataM vachaH || 10.50.6
ye te vipra brahmakR^itaH sute sachA vasUnAM cha vasunashcha dAvane |pra te sumnasya manasA pathA bhuvanmade sutasya somyasyAndhasaH || 10.50.7

mahattadulbaM sthaviraM tadAsIdyenAviShTitaH praviveshithApaH |vishvA apashyadbahudhA te agne jAtavedastanvo deva ekaH || 10.51.1
ko mA dadarsha katamaH sa devo yo me tanvo bahudhA paryapashyat |kvAha mitrAvaruNA kShiyantyagnervishvAH samidho devayAnIH || 10.51.2
aichChAma tvA bahudhA jAtavedaH praviShTamagne apsvoShadhIShu |taM tvA yamo achikechchitrabhAno dashAntaruShyAdatirochamAnam || 10.51.3
hotrAdahaM varuNa bibhyadAyaM nedeva mA yunajannatra devAH |tasya me tanvo bahudhA niviShTA etamarthaM na chiketAhamagniH || 10.51.4
ehi manurdevayuryaj~nakAmo.araMkR^ityA tamasi kSheShyagne |sugAnpathaH kR^iNuhi devayAnAnvaha havyAni sumanasyamAnaH || 10.51.5
agneH pUrve bhrAtaro arthametaM rathIvAdhvAnamanvAvarIvuH |tasmAdbhiyA varuNa dUramAyaM gauro na kShepnoravije jyAyAH || 10.51.6
kurmasta AyurajaraM yadagne yathA yukto jAtavedo na riShyAH |athA vahAsi sumanasyamAno bhAgaM devebhyo haviShaH sujAta || 10.51.7
prayAjAnme anuyAjA.Nshcha kevalAnUrjasvantaM haviSho datta bhAgam |ghR^itaM chApAM puruShaM chauShadhInAmagneshcha dIrghamAyurastu devAH || 10.51.8
tava prayAjA anuyAjAshcha kevala Urjasvanto haviShaH santu bhAgAH |tavAgne yaj~no.ayamastu sarvastubhyaM namantAM pradishashchatasraH || 10.51.9

vishve devAH shAstana mA yatheha hotA vR^ito manavai yanniShadya |pra me brUta bhAgadheyaM yathA vo yena pathA havyamA vo vahAni || 10.52.1
ahaM hotA nyasIdaM yajIyAnvishve devA maruto mA junanti |aharaharashvinAdhvaryavaM vAM brahmA samidbhavati sAhutirvAm || 10.52.2
ayaM yo hotA kiru sa yamasya kamapyUhe yatsama~njanti devAH |aharaharjAyate mAsimAsyathA devA dadhire havyavAham || 10.52.3
mAM devA dadhire havyavAhamapamluktaM bahu kR^ichChrA charantam |agnirvidvAnyaj~naM naH kalpayAti pa~nchayAmaM trivR^itaM saptatantum || 10.52.4
A vo yakShyamR^itatvaM suvIraM yathA vo devA varivaH karANi |A bAhvorvajramindrasya dheyAmathemA vishvAH pR^itanA jayAti || 10.52.5
trINi shatA trI sahasrANyagniM triMshachcha devA nava chAsaparyan |aukShanghR^itairastR^iNanbarhirasmA AdiddhotAraM nyasAdayanta || 10.52.6

yamaichChAma manasA so.ayamAgAdyaj~nasya vidvAnparuShashchikitvAn |sa no yakShaddevatAtA yajIyAnni hi ShatsadantaraH pUrvo asmat || 10.53.1
arAdhi hotA niShadA yajIyAnabhi prayAMsi sudhitAni hi khyat |yajAmahai yaj~niyAnhanta devA.N ILAmahA IDyA.N Ajyena || 10.53.2
sAdhvImakardevavItiM no adya yaj~nasya jihvAmavidAma guhyAm |sa AyurAgAtsurabhirvasAno bhadrAmakardevahUtiM no adya || 10.53.3
tadadya vAchaH prathamaM masIya yenAsurA.N abhi devA asAma |UrjAda uta yaj~niyAsaH pa~ncha janA mama hotraM juShadhvam || 10.53.4
pa~ncha janA mama hotraM juShantAM gojAtA uta ye yaj~niyAsaH |pR^ithivI naH pArthivAtpAtvaMhaso.antarikShaM divyAtpAtvasmAn || 10.53.5
tantuM tanvanrajaso bhAnumanvihi jyotiShmataH patho rakSha dhiyA kR^itAn |anulbaNaM vayata joguvAmapo manurbhava janayA daivyaM janam || 10.53.6
akShAnaho nahyatanota somyA iShkR^iNudhvaM rashanA ota piMshata |aShTAvandhuraM vahatAbhito rathaM yena devAso anayannabhi priyam || 10.53.7
ashmanvatI rIyate saM rabhadhvamuttiShThata pra taratA sakhAyaH |atrA jahAma ye asannashevAH shivAnvayamuttaremAbhi vAjAn || 10.53.8
tvaShTA mAyA vedapasAmapastamo bibhratpAtrA devapAnAni shaMtamA |shishIte nUnaM parashuM svAyasaM yena vR^ishchAdetasho brahmaNaspatiH || 10.53.9
sato nUnaM kavayaH saM shishIta vAshIbhiryAbhiramR^itAya takShatha |vidvAMsaH padA guhyAni kartana yena devAso amR^itatvamAnashuH || 10.53.10
garbhe yoShAmadadhurvatsamAsanyapIchyena manasota jihvayA |sa vishvAhA sumanA yogyA abhi siShAsanirvanate kAra ijjitim || 10.53.11

tAM su te kIrtiM maghavanmahitvA yattvA bhIte rodasI ahvayetAm |prAvo devA.N Atiro dAsamojaH prajAyai tvasyai yadashikSha indra || 10.54.1
yadacharastanvA vAvR^idhAno balAnIndra prabruvANo janeShu |mAyetsA te yAni yuddhAnyAhurnAdya shatruM nanu purA vivitse || 10.54.2
ka u nu te mahimanaH samasyAsmatpUrva R^iShayo.antamApuH |yanmAtaraM cha pitaraM cha sAkamajanayathAstanvaH svAyAH || 10.54.3
chatvAri te asuryANi nAmAdAbhyAni mahiShasya santi |tvama~Nga tAni vishvAni vitse yebhiH karmANi maghava~nchakartha || 10.54.4
tvaM vishvA dadhiShe kevalAni yAnyAviryA cha guhA vasUni |kAmaminme maghavanmA vi tArIstvamAj~nAtA tvamindrAsi dAtA || 10.54.5
yo adadhAjjyotiShi jyotirantaryo asR^ijanmadhunA saM madhUni |adha priyaM shUShamindrAya manma brahmakR^ito bR^ihadukthAdavAchi || 10.54.6

dUre tannAma guhyaM parAchairyattvA bhIte ahvayetAM vayodhai |udastabhnAH pR^ithivIM dyAmabhIke bhrAtuH putrAnmaghavantitviShANaH || 10.55.1
mahattannAma guhyaM puruspR^igyena bhUtaM janayo yena bhavyam |pratnaM jAtaM jyotiryadasya priyaM priyAH samavishanta pa~ncha || 10.55.2
A rodasI apR^iNAdota madhyaM pa~ncha devA.N R^itushaH saptasapta |chatustriMshatA purudhA vi chaShTe sarUpeNa jyotiShA vivratena || 10.55.3
yaduSha auchChaH prathamA vibhAnAmajanayo yena puShTasya puShTam |yatte jAmitvamavaraM parasyA mahanmahatyA asuratvamekam || 10.55.4
vidhuM dadrANaM samane bahUnAM yuvAnaM santaM palito jagAra |devasya pashya kAvyaM mahitvAdyA mamAra sa hyaH samAna || 10.55.5
shAkmanA shAko aruNaH suparNa A yo mahaH shUraH sanAdanILaH |yachchiketa satyamittanna moghaM vasu spArhamuta jetota dAtA || 10.55.6
aibhirdade vR^iShNyA pauMsyAni yebhiraukShadvR^itrahatyAya vajrI |ye karmaNaH kriyamANasya mahna R^itekarmamudajAyanta devAH || 10.55.7
yujA karmANi janayanvishvaujA ashastihA vishvamanAsturAShAT |pItvI somasya diva A vR^idhAnaH shUro niryudhAdhamaddasyUn || 10.55.8

idaM ta ekaM para U ta ekaM tR^itIyena jyotiShA saM vishasva |saMveshane tanvashchAruredhi priyo devAnAM parame janitre || 10.56.1
tanUShTe vAjintanvaM nayantI vAmamasmabhyaM dhAtu sharma tubhyam |ahruto maho dharuNAya devAndivIva jyotiH svamA mimIyAH || 10.56.2
vAjyasi vAjinenA suvenIH suvitaH stomaM suvito divaM gAH |suvito dharma prathamAnu satyA suvito devAnsuvito.anu patma || 10.56.3
mahimna eShAM pitarashchaneshire devA deveShvadadhurapi kratum |samavivyachuruta yAnyatviShuraiShAM tanUShu ni vivishuH punaH || 10.56.4
sahobhirvishvaM pari chakramU rajaH pUrvA dhAmAnyamitA mimAnAH |tanUShu vishvA bhuvanA ni yemire prAsArayanta purudha prajA anu || 10.56.5
dvidhA sUnavo.asuraM svarvidamAsthApayanta tR^itIyena karmaNA |svAM prajAM pitaraH pitryaM saha AvareShvadadhustantumAtatam || 10.56.6
nAvA na kShodaH pradishaH pR^ithivyAH svastibhirati durgANi vishvA |svAM prajAM bR^ihaduktho mahitvAvareShvadadhAdA pareShu || 10.56.7

mA pra gAma patho vayaM mA yaj~nAdindra sominaH |mAntaH sthurno arAtayaH || 10.57.1
yo yaj~nasya prasAdhanastanturdeveShvAtataH |tamAhutaM nashImahi || 10.57.2
mano nvA huvAmahe nArAshaMsena somena |pitR^INAM cha manmabhiH || 10.57.3
A ta etu manaH punaH kratve dakShAya jIvase |jyokcha sUryaM dR^ishe || 10.57.4
punarnaH pitaro mano dadAtu daivyo janaH |jIvaM vrAtaM sachemahi || 10.57.5
vayaM soma vrate tava manastanUShu bibhrataH |prajAvantaH sachemahi || 10.57.6

yatte yamaM vaivasvataM mano jagAma dUrakam |tatta A vartayAmasIha kShayAya jIvase || 10.58.1
yatte divaM yatpR^ithivIM mano jagAma dUrakam |tatta A vartayAmasIha kShayAya jIvase || 10.58.2
yatte bhUmiM chaturbhR^iShTiM mano jagAma dUrakam |tatta A vartayAmasIha kShayAya jIvase || 10.58.3
yatte chatasraH pradisho mano jagAma dUrakam |tatta A vartayAmasIha kShayAya jIvase || 10.58.4
yatte samudramarNavaM mano jagAma dUrakam |tatta A vartayAmasIha kShayAya jIvase || 10.58.5
yatte marIchIH pravato mano jagAma dUrakam |tatta A vartayAmasIha kShayAya jIvase || 10.58.6
yatte apo yadoShadhIrmano jagAma dUrakam |tatta A vartayAmasIha kShayAya jIvase || 10.58.7
yatte sUryaM yaduShasaM mano jagAma dUrakam |tatta A vartayAmasIha kShayAya jIvase || 10.58.8
yatte parvatAnbR^ihato mano jagAma dUrakam |tatta A vartayAmasIha kShayAya jIvase || 10.58.9
yatte vishvamidaM jaganmano jagAma dUrakam |tatta A vartayAmasIha kShayAya jIvase || 10.58.10
yatte parAH parAvato mano jagAma dUrakam |tatta A vartayAmasIha kShayAya jIvase || 10.58.11
yatte bhUtaM cha bhavyaM cha mano jagAma dUrakam |tatta A vartayAmasIha kShayAya jIvase || 10.58.12

pra tAryAyuH prataraM navIyaH sthAtAreva kratumatA rathasya |adha chyavAna uttavItyarthaM parAtaraM su nirR^itirjihItAm || 10.59.1
sAmannu rAye nidhimannvannaM karAmahe su purudha shravAMsi |tA no vishvAni jaritA mamattu parAtaraM su nirR^itirjihItAm || 10.59.2
abhI ShvaryaH pauMsyairbhavema dyaurna bhUmiM girayo nAjrAn |tA no vishvAni jaritA chiketa parAtaraM su nirR^itirjihItAm || 10.59.3
mo Shu NaH soma mR^ityave parA dAH pashyema nu sUryamuchcharantam |dyubhirhito jarimA sU no astu parAtaraM su nirR^itirjihItAm || 10.59.4
asunIte mano asmAsu dhAraya jIvAtave su pra tirA na AyuH |rArandhi naH sUryasya saMdR^ishi ghR^itena tvaM tanvaM vardhayasva || 10.59.5
asunIte punarasmAsu chakShuH punaH prANamiha no dhehi bhogam |jyokpashyema sUryamuchcharantamanumate mR^iLayA naH svasti || 10.59.6
punarno asuM pR^ithivI dadAtu punardyaurdevI punarantarikSham |punarnaH somastanvaM dadAtu punaH pUShA pathyAM yA svastiH || 10.59.7
shaM rodasI subandhave yahvI R^itasya mAtarA |bharatAmapa yadrapo dyauH pR^ithivi kShamA rapo mo Shu te kiM chanAmamat || 10.59.8
ava dvake ava trikA divashcharanti bheShajA |kShamA chariShNvekakaM bharatAmapa yadrapo dyauH pR^ithivi kShamA rapo mo Shu te kiM chanAmamat || 10.59.9
samindreraya gAmanaDvAhaM ya AvahadushInarANyA anaH |bharatAmapa yadrapo dyauH pR^ithivi kShamA rapo mo Shu te kiM chanAmamat || 10.59.10

A janaM tveShasaMdR^ishaM mAhInAnAmupastutam |aganma bibhrato namaH || 10.60.1
asamAtiM nitoshanaM tveShaM niyayinaM ratham |bhajerathasya satpatim || 10.60.2
yo janAnmahiShA.N ivAtitasthau pavIravAn |utApavIravAnyudhA || 10.60.3
yasyekShvAkurupa vrate revAnmarAyyedhate |divIva pa~ncha kR^iShTayaH || 10.60.4
indra kShatrAsamAtiShu rathaproShTheShu dhAraya |divIva sUryaM dR^ishe || 10.60.5
agastyasya nadbhyaH saptI yunakShi rohitA |paNInnyakramIrabhi vishvAnrAjannarAdhasaH || 10.60.6
ayaM mAtAyaM pitAyaM jIvAturAgamat |idaM tava prasarpaNaM subandhavehi nirihi || 10.60.7
yathA yugaM varatrayA nahyanti dharuNAya kam |evA dAdhAra te mano jIvAtave na mR^ityave.atho ariShTatAtaye || 10.60.8
yatheyaM pR^ithivI mahI dAdhAremAnvanaspatIn |evA dAdhAra te mano jIvAtave na mR^ityave.atho ariShTatAtaye || 10.60.9
yamAdahaM vaivasvatAtsubandhormana Abharam |jIvAtave na mR^ityave.atho ariShTatAtaye || 10.60.10
nyagvAto.ava vAti nyaktapati sUryaH |nIchInamaghnyA duhe nyagbhavatu te rapaH || 10.60.11
ayaM me hasto bhagavAnayaM me bhagavattaraH |ayaM me vishvabheShajo.ayaM shivAbhimarshanaH || 10.60.12

idamitthA raudraM gUrtavachA brahma kratvA shachyAmantarAjau |krANA yadasya pitarA maMhaneShThAH parShatpakthe ahannA sapta hotR^In || 10.61.1
sa iddAnAya dabhyAya vanva~nchyavAnaH sUdairamimIta vedim |tUrvayANo gUrtavachastamaH kShodo na reta ita/Uti si~nchat || 10.61.2
mano na yeShu havaneShu tigmaM vipaH shachyA vanutho dravantA |A yaH sharyAbhistuvinR^imNo asyAshrINItAdishaM gabhastau || 10.61.3
kR^iShNA yadgoShvaruNIShu sIdaddivo napAtAshvinA huve vAm |vItaM me yaj~namA gataM me annaM vavanvAMsA neShamasmR^itadhrU || 10.61.4
prathiShTa yasya vIrakarmamiShNadanuShThitaM nu naryo apauhat |punastadA vR^ihati yatkanAyA duhiturA anubhR^itamanarvA || 10.61.5
madhyA yatkartvamabhavadabhIke kAmaM kR^iNvAne pitari yuvatyAm |manAnagreto jahaturviyantA sAnau niShiktaM sukR^itasya yonau || 10.61.6
pitA yatsvAM duhitaramadhiShkankShmayA retaH saMjagmAno ni Shi~nchat |svAdhyo.ajanayanbrahma devA vAstoShpatiM vratapAM niratakShan || 10.61.7
sa IM vR^iShA na phenamasyadAjau smadA paraidapa dabhrachetAH |saratpadA na dakShiNA parAvR^i~Nna tA nu me pR^ishanyo jagR^ibhre || 10.61.8
makShU na vahniH prajAyA upabdiragniM na nagna upa sIdadUdhaH |sanitedhmaM sanitota vAjaM sa dhartA jaj~ne sahasA yavIyut || 10.61.9
makShU kanAyAH sakhyaM navagvA R^itaM vadanta R^itayuktimagman |dvibarhaso ya upa gopamAguradakShiNAso achyutA dudukShan || 10.61.10
makShU kanAyAH sakhyaM navIyo rAdho na reta R^itamitturaNyan |shuchi yatte rekNa Ayajanta sabardughAyAH paya usriyAyAH || 10.61.11
pashvA yatpashchA viyutA budhanteti bravIti vaktarI rarANaH |vasorvasutvA kAravo.anehA vishvaM viveShTi draviNamupa kShu || 10.61.12
tadinnvasya pariShadvAno agmanpurU sadanto nArShadaM bibhitsan |vi shuShNasya saMgrathitamanarvA vidatpuruprajAtasya guhA yat || 10.61.13
bhargo ha nAmota yasya devAH svarNa ye triShadhasthe niSheduH |agnirha nAmota jAtavedAH shrudhI no hotarR^itasya hotAdhruk || 10.61.14
uta tyA me raudrAvarchimantA nAsatyAvindra gUrtaye yajadhyai |manuShvadvR^iktabarhiShe rarANA mandU hitaprayasA vikShu yajyU || 10.61.15
ayaM stuto rAjA vandi vedhA apashcha viprastarati svasetuH |sa kakShIvantaM rejayatso agniM nemiM na chakramarvato raghudru || 10.61.16
sa dvibandhurvaitaraNo yaShTA sabardhuM dhenumasvaM duhadhyai |saM yanmitrAvaruNA vR^i~nja ukthairjyeShThebhiraryamaNaM varUthaiH || 10.61.17
tadbandhuH sUrirdivi te dhiyaMdhA nAbhAnediShTho rapati pra venan |sA no nAbhiH paramAsya vA ghAhaM tatpashchA katithashchidAsa || 10.61.18
iyaM me nAbhiriha me sadhasthamime me devA ayamasmi sarvaH |dvijA aha prathamajA R^itasyedaM dhenuraduhajjAyamAnA || 10.61.19
adhAsu mandro aratirvibhAvAva syati dvivartanirvaneShAT |UrdhvA yachChreNirna shishurdanmakShU sthiraM shevR^idhaM sUta mAtA || 10.61.20
adhA gAva upamAtiM kanAyA anu shvAntasya kasya chitpareyuH |shrudhi tvaM sudraviNo nastvaM yALAshvaghnasya vAvR^idhe sUnR^itAbhiH || 10.61.21
adha tvamindra viddhyasmAnmaho rAye nR^ipate vajrabAhuH |rakShA cha no maghonaH pAhi sUrInanehasaste harivo abhiShTau || 10.61.22
adha yadrAjAnA gaviShTau saratsaraNyuH kArave jaraNyuH |vipraH preShThaH sa hyeShAM babhUva parA cha vakShaduta parShadenAn || 10.61.23
adhA nvasya jenyasya puShTau vR^ithA rebhanta Imahe tadU nu |saraNyurasya sUnurashvo viprashchAsi shravasashcha sAtau || 10.61.24
yuvoryadi sakhyAyAsme shardhAya stomaM jujuShe namasvAn |vishvatra yasminnA giraH samIchIH pUrvIva gAturdAshatsUnR^itAyai || 10.61.25
sa gR^iNAno adbhirdevavAniti subandhurnamasA sUktaiH |vardhadukthairvachobhirA hi nUnaM vyadhvaiti payasa usriyAyAH || 10.61.26
ta U Shu No maho yajatrA bhUta devAsa Utaye sajoShAH |ye vAjA.N anayatA viyanto ye sthA nichetAro amUrAH || 10.61.27

ye yaj~nena dakShiNayA samaktA indrasya sakhyamamR^itatvamAnasha |tebhyo bhadrama~Ngiraso vo astu prati gR^ibhNIta mAnavaM sumedhasaH || 10.62.1
ya udAjanpitaro gomayaM vasvR^itenAbhindanparivatsare valam |dIrghAyutvama~Ngiraso vo astu prati gR^ibhNIta mAnavaM sumedhasaH || 10.62.2
ya R^itena sUryamArohayandivyaprathayanpR^ithivIM mAtaraM vi |suprajAstvama~Ngiraso vo astu prati gR^ibhNIta mAnavaM sumedhasaH || 10.62.3
ayaM nAbhA vadati valgu vo gR^ihe devaputrA R^iShayastachChR^iNotana |subrahmaNyama~Ngiraso vo astu prati gR^ibhNIta mAnavaM sumedhasaH || 10.62.4
virUpAsa idR^iShayasta idgambhIravepasaH |te a~NgirasaH sUnavaste agneH pari jaj~nire || 10.62.5
ye agneH pari jaj~nire virUpAso divaspari |navagvo nu dashagvo a~Ngirastamo sachA deveShu maMhate || 10.62.6
indreNa yujA niH sR^ijanta vAghato vrajaM gomantamashvinam |sahasraM me dadato aShTakarNyaH shravo deveShvakrata || 10.62.7
pra nUnaM jAyatAmayaM manustokmeva rohatu |yaH sahasraM shatAshvaM sadyo dAnAya maMhate || 10.62.8
na tamashnoti kashchana diva iva sAnvArabham |sAvarNyasya dakShiNA vi sindhuriva paprathe || 10.62.9
uta dAsA pariviShe smaddiShTI goparINasA |yadusturvashcha mAmahe || 10.62.10
sahasradA grAmaNIrmA riShanmanuH sUryeNAsya yatamAnaitu dakShiNA |sAvarNerdevAH pra tirantvAyuryasminnashrAntA asanAma vAjam || 10.62.11

parAvato ye didhiShanta ApyaM manuprItAso janimA vivasvataH |yayAterye nahuShyasya barhiShi devA Asate te adhi bruvantu naH || 10.63.1
vishvA hi vo namasyAni vandyA nAmAni devA uta yaj~niyAni vaH |ye stha jAtA aditeradbhyaspari ye pR^ithivyAste ma iha shrutA havam || 10.63.2
yebhyo mAtA madhumatpinvate payaH pIyUShaM dyauraditiradribarhAH |ukthashuShmAnvR^iShabharAnsvapnasastA.N AdityA.N anu madA svastaye || 10.63.3
nR^ichakShaso animiShanto arhaNA bR^ihaddevAso amR^itatvamAnashuH |jyotIrathA ahimAyA anAgaso divo varShmANaM vasate svastaye || 10.63.4
samrAjo ye suvR^idho yaj~namAyayuraparihvR^itA dadhire divi kShayam |tA.N A vivAsa namasA suvR^iktibhirmaho AdityA.N aditiM svastaye || 10.63.5
ko vaH stomaM rAdhati yaM jujoShatha vishve devAso manuSho yati ShThana |ko vo.adhvaraM tuvijAtA araM karadyo naH parShadatyaMhaH svastaye || 10.63.6
yebhyo hotrAM prathamAmAyeje manuH samiddhAgnirmanasA sapta hotR^ibhiH |ta AdityA abhayaM sharma yachChata sugA naH karta supathA svastaye || 10.63.7
ya Ishire bhuvanasya prachetaso vishvasya sthAturjagatashcha mantavaH |te naH kR^itAdakR^itAdenasasparyadyA devAsaH pipR^itA svastaye || 10.63.8
bhareShvindraM suhavaM havAmaheM.ahomuchaM sukR^itaM daivyaM janam |agniM mitraM varuNaM sAtaye bhagaM dyAvApR^ithivI marutaH svastaye || 10.63.9
sutrAmANaM pR^ithivIM dyAmanehasaM susharmANamaditiM supraNItim |daivIM nAvaM svaritrAmanAgasamasravantImA ruhemA svastaye || 10.63.10
vishve yajatrA adhi vochatotaye trAyadhvaM no durevAyA abhihrutaH |satyayA vo devahUtyA huvema shR^iNvato devA avase svastaye || 10.63.11
apAmIvAmapa vishvAmanAhutimapArAtiM durvidatrAmaghAyataH |Are devA dveSho asmadyuyotanoru NaH sharma yachChatA svastaye || 10.63.12
ariShTaH sa marto vishva edhate pra prajAbhirjAyate dharmaNaspari |yamAdityAso nayathA sunItibhirati vishvAni duritA svastaye || 10.63.13
yaM devAso.avatha vAjasAtau yaM shUrasAtA maruto hite dhane |prAtaryAvANaM rathamindra sAnasimariShyantamA ruhemA svastaye || 10.63.14
svasti naH pathyAsu dhanvasu svastyapsu vR^ijane svarvati |svasti naH putrakR^itheShu yoniShu svasti rAye maruto dadhAtana || 10.63.15
svastiriddhi prapathe shreShThA rekNasvatyabhi yA vAmameti |sA no amA so araNe ni pAtu svAveshA bhavatu devagopA || 10.63.16
evA plateH sUnuravIvR^idhadvo vishva AdityA adite manIShI |IshAnAso naro amartyenAstAvi jano divyo gayena || 10.63.17

kathA devAnAM katamasya yAmani sumantu nAma shR^iNvatAM manAmahe |ko mR^iLAti katamo no mayaskaratkatama UtI abhyA vavartati || 10.64.1
kratUyanti kratavo hR^itsu dhItayo venanti venAH patayantyA dishaH |na marDitA vidyate anya ebhyo deveShu me adhi kAmA ayaMsata || 10.64.2
narA vA shaMsaM pUShaNamagohyamagniM deveddhamabhyarchase girA |sUryAmAsA chandramasA yamaM divi tritaM vAtamuShasamaktumashvinA || 10.64.3
kathA kavistuvIravAnkayA girA bR^ihaspatirvAvR^idhate suvR^iktibhiH |aja ekapAtsuhavebhirR^ikvabhirahiH shR^iNotu budhnyo havImani || 10.64.4
dakShasya vAdite janmani vrate rAjAnA mitrAvaruNA vivAsasi |atUrtapanthAH pururatho aryamA saptahotA viShurUpeShu janmasu || 10.64.5
te no arvanto havanashruto havaM vishve shR^iNvantu vAjino mitadravaH |sahasrasA medhasAtAviva tmanA maho ye dhanaM samitheShu jabhrire || 10.64.6
pra vo vAyuM rathayujaM puraMdhiM stomaiH kR^iNudhvaM sakhyAya pUShaNam |te hi devasya savituH savImani kratuM sachante sachitaH sachetasaH || 10.64.7
triH sapta sasrA nadyo mahIrapo vanaspatInparvatA.N agnimUtaye |kR^ishAnumastR^IntiShyaM sadhastha A rudraM rudreShu rudriyaM havAmahe || 10.64.8
sarasvatI sarayuH sindhurUrmibhirmaho mahIravasA yantu vakShaNIH |devIrApo mAtaraH sUdayitnvo ghR^itavatpayo madhumanno archata || 10.64.9
uta mAtA bR^ihaddivA shR^iNotu nastvaShTA devebhirjanibhiH pitA vachaH |R^ibhukShA vAjo rathaspatirbhago raNvaH shaMsaH shashamAnasya pAtu naH || 10.64.10
raNvaH saMdR^iShTau pitumA.N iva kShayo bhadrA rudrANAM marutAmupastutiH |gobhiH ShyAma yashaso janeShvA sadA devAsa iLayA sachemahi || 10.64.11
yAM me dhiyaM maruta indra devA adadAta varuNa mitra yUyam |tAM pIpayata payaseva dhenuM kuvidgiro adhi rathe vahAtha || 10.64.12
kuvida~Nga prati yathA chidasya naH sajAtyasya maruto bubodhatha |nAbhA yatra prathamaM saMnasAmahe tatra jAmitvamaditirdadhAtu naH || 10.64.13
te hi dyAvApR^ithivI mAtarA mahI devI devA~njanmanA yaj~niye itaH |ubhe bibhR^ita ubhayaM bharImabhiH purU retAMsi pitR^ibhishcha si~nchataH || 10.64.14
vi ShA hotrA vishvamashnoti vAryaM bR^ihaspatiraramatiH panIyasI |grAvA yatra madhuShuduchyate bR^ihadavIvashanta matibhirmanIShiNaH || 10.64.15
evA kavistuvIravA.N R^itaj~nA draviNasyurdraviNasashchakAnaH |ukthebhiratra matibhishcha vipro.apIpayadgayo divyAni janma || 10.64.16
evA plateH sUnuravIvR^idhadvo vishva AdityA adite manIShI |IshAnAso naro amartyenAstAvi jano divyo gayena || 10.64.17

agnirindro varuNo mitro aryamA vAyuH pUShA sarasvatI sajoShasaH |AdityA viShNurmarutaH svarbR^ihatsomo rudro aditirbrahmaNaspatiH || 10.65.1
indrAgnI vR^itrahatyeShu satpatI mitho hinvAnA tanvA samokasA |antarikShaM mahyA paprurojasA somo ghR^itashrIrmahimAnamIrayan || 10.65.2
teShAM hi mahnA mahatAmanarvaNAM stomA.N iyarmyR^itaj~nA R^itAvR^idhAm |ye apsavamarNavaM chitrarAdhasaste no rAsantAM mahaye sumitryAH || 10.65.3
svarNaramantarikShANi rochanA dyAvAbhUmI pR^ithivIM skambhurojasA |pR^ikShA iva mahayantaH surAtayo devAH stavante manuShAya sUrayaH || 10.65.4
mitrAya shikSha varuNAya dAshuShe yA samrAjA manasA na prayuchChataH |yayordhAma dharmaNA rochate bR^ihadyayorubhe rodasI nAdhasI vR^itau || 10.65.5
yA gaurvartaniM paryeti niShkR^itaM payo duhAnA vratanIravArataH |sA prabruvANA varuNAya dAshuShe devebhyo dAshaddhaviShA vivasvate || 10.65.6
divakShaso agnijihvA R^itAvR^idha R^itasya yoniM vimR^ishanta Asate |dyAM skabhitvyapa A chakrurojasA yaj~naM janitvI tanvI ni mAmR^ijuH || 10.65.7
parikShitA pitarA pUrvajAvarI R^itasya yonA kShayataH samokasA |dyAvApR^ithivI varuNAya savrate ghR^itavatpayo mahiShAya pinvataH || 10.65.8
parjanyAvAtA vR^iShabhA purIShiNendravAyU varuNo mitro aryamA |devA.N AdityA.N aditiM havAmahe ye pArthivAso divyAso apsu ye || 10.65.9
tvaShTAraM vAyumR^ibhavo ya ohate daivyA hotArA uShasaM svastaye |bR^ihaspatiM vR^itrakhAdaM sumedhasamindriyaM somaM dhanasA u Imahe || 10.65.10
brahma gAmashvaM janayanta oShadhIrvanaspatInpR^ithivIM parvatA.N apaH |sUryaM divi rohayantaH sudAnava AryA vratA visR^ijanto adhi kShami || 10.65.11
bhujyumaMhasaH pipR^itho nirashvinA shyAvaM putraM vadhrimatyA ajinvatam |kamadyuvaM vimadAyohathuryuvaM viShNApvaM vishvakAyAva sR^ijathaH || 10.65.12
pAvIravI tanyaturekapAdajo divo dhartA sindhurApaH samudriyaH |vishve devAsaH shR^iNavanvachAMsi me sarasvatI saha dhIbhiH puraMdhyA || 10.65.13
vishve devAH saha dhIbhiH puraMdhyA manoryajatrA amR^itA R^itaj~nAH |rAtiShAcho abhiShAchaH svarvidaH svargiro brahma sUktaM juSherata || 10.65.14
devAnvasiShTho amR^itAnvavande ye vishvA bhuvanAbhi pratasthuH |te no rAsantAmurugAyamadya yUyaM pAta svastibhiH sadA naH || 10.65.15

devAnhuve bR^ihachChravasaH svastaye jyotiShkR^ito adhvarasya prachetasaH |ye vAvR^idhuH prataraM vishvavedasa indrajyeShThAso amR^itA R^itAvR^idhaH || 10.66.1
indraprasUtA varuNaprashiShTA ye sUryasya jyotiSho bhAgamAnashuH |marudgaNe vR^ijane manma dhImahi mAghone yaj~naM janayanta sUrayaH || 10.66.2
indro vasubhiH pari pAtu no gayamAdityairno aditiH sharma yachChatu |rudro rudrebhirdevo mR^iLayAti nastvaShTA no gnAbhiH suvitAya jinvatu || 10.66.3
aditirdyAvApR^ithivI R^itaM mahadindrAviShNU marutaH svarbR^ihat |devA.N AdityA.N avase havAmahe vasUnrudrAnsavitAraM sudaMsasam || 10.66.4
sarasvAndhIbhirvaruNo dhR^itavrataH pUShA viShNurmahimA vAyurashvinA |brahmakR^ito amR^itA vishvavedasaH sharma no yaMsantrivarUthamaMhasaH || 10.66.5
vR^iShA yaj~no vR^iShaNaH santu yaj~niyA vR^iShaNo devA vR^iShaNo haviShkR^itaH |vR^iShaNA dyAvApR^ithivI R^itAvarI vR^iShA parjanyo vR^iShaNo vR^iShastubhaH || 10.66.6
agnIShomA vR^iShaNA vAjasAtaye puruprashastA vR^iShaNA upa bruve |yAvIjire vR^iShaNo devayajyayA tA naH sharma trivarUthaM vi yaMsataH || 10.66.7
dhR^itavratAH kShatriyA yaj~naniShkR^ito bR^ihaddivA adhvarANAmabhishriyaH |agnihotAra R^itasApo adruho.apo asR^ijannanu vR^itratUrye || 10.66.8
dyAvApR^ithivI janayannabhi vratApa oShadhIrvaninAni yaj~niyA |antarikShaM svarA paprurUtaye vashaM devAsastanvI ni mAmR^ijuH || 10.66.9
dhartAro diva R^ibhavaH suhastA vAtAparjanyA mahiShasya tanyatoH |Apa oShadhIH pra tirantu no giro bhago rAtirvAjino yantu me havam || 10.66.10
samudraH sindhU rajo antarikShamaja ekapAttanayitnurarNavaH |ahirbudhnyaH shR^iNavadvachAMsi me vishve devAsa uta sUrayo mama || 10.66.11
syAma vo manavo devavItaye prA~nchaM no yaj~naM pra Nayata sAdhuyA |AdityA rudrA vasavaH sudAnava imA brahma shasyamAnAni jinvata || 10.66.12
daivyA hotArA prathamA purohita R^itasya panthAmanvemi sAdhuyA |kShetrasya patiM prativeshamImahe vishvAndevA.N amR^itA.N aprayuchChataH || 10.66.13
vasiShThAsaH pitR^ivadvAchamakrata devA.N ILAnA R^iShivatsvastaye |prItA iva j~nAtayaH kAmametyAsme devAso.ava dhUnutA vasu || 10.66.14
devAnvasiShTho amR^itAnvavande ye vishvA bhuvanAbhi pratasthuH |te no rAsantAmurugAyamadya yUyaM pAta svastibhiH sadA naH || 10.66.15

imAM dhiyaM saptashIrShNIM pitA na R^itaprajAtAM bR^ihatImavindat |turIyaM svijjanayadvishvajanyo.ayAsya ukthamindrAya shaMsan || 10.67.1
R^itaM shaMsanta R^iju dIdhyAnA divasputrAso asurasya vIrAH |vipraM padama~Ngiraso dadhAnA yaj~nasya dhAma prathamaM mananta || 10.67.2
haMsairiva sakhibhirvAvadadbhirashmanmayAni nahanA vyasyan |bR^ihaspatirabhikanikradadgA uta prAstauduchcha vidvA.N agAyat || 10.67.3
avo dvAbhyAM para ekayA gA guhA tiShThantIranR^itasya setau |bR^ihaspatistamasi jyotirichChannudusrA Akarvi hi tisra AvaH || 10.67.4
vibhidyA puraM shayathemapAchIM nistrINi sAkamudadherakR^intat |bR^ihaspatiruShasaM sUryaM gAmarkaM viveda stanayanniva dyauH || 10.67.5
indro valaM rakShitAraM dughAnAM kareNeva vi chakartA raveNa |svedA~njibhirAshiramichChamAno.arodayatpaNimA gA amuShNAt || 10.67.6
sa IM satyebhiH sakhibhiH shuchadbhirgodhAyasaM vi dhanasairadardaH |brahmaNaspatirvR^iShabhirvarAhairgharmasvedebhirdraviNaM vyAnaT || 10.67.7
te satyena manasA gopatiM gA iyAnAsa iShaNayanta dhIbhiH |bR^ihaspatirmitho/avadyapebhirudusriyA asR^ijata svayugbhiH || 10.67.8
taM vardhayanto matibhiH shivAbhiH siMhamiva nAnadataM sadhasthe |bR^ihaspatiM vR^iShaNaM shUrasAtau bharebhare anu madema jiShNum || 10.67.9
yadA vAjamasanadvishvarUpamA dyAmarukShaduttarANi sadma |bR^ihaspatiM vR^iShaNaM vardhayanto nAnA santo bibhrato jyotirAsA || 10.67.10
satyAmAshiShaM kR^iNutA vayodhai kIriM chiddhyavatha svebhirevaiH |pashchA mR^idho apa bhavantu vishvAstadrodasI shR^iNutaM vishvaminve || 10.67.11
indro mahnA mahato arNavasya vi mUrdhAnamabhinadarbudasya |ahannahimariNAtsapta sindhUndevairdyAvApR^ithivI prAvataM naH || 10.67.12

udapruto na vayo rakShamANA vAvadato abhriyasyeva ghoShAH |giribhrajo normayo madanto bR^ihaspatimabhyarkA anAvan || 10.68.1
saM gobhirA~Ngiraso nakShamANo bhaga ivedaryamaNaM ninAya |jane mitro na dampatI anakti bR^ihaspate vAjayAshU.NrivAjau || 10.68.2
sAdhvaryA atithinIriShirAH spArhAH suvarNA anavadyarUpAH |bR^ihaspatiH parvatebhyo vitUryA nirgA Upe yavamiva sthivibhyaH || 10.68.3
ApruShAyanmadhuna R^itasya yonimavakShipannarka ulkAmiva dyoH |bR^ihaspatiruddharannashmano gA bhUmyA udneva vi tvachaM bibheda || 10.68.4
apa jyotiShA tamo antarikShAdudnaH shIpAlamiva vAta Ajat |bR^ihaspatiranumR^ishyA valasyAbhramiva vAta A chakra A gAH || 10.68.5
yadA valasya pIyato jasuM bhedbR^ihaspatiragnitapobhirarkaiH |dadbhirna jihvA pariviShTamAdadAvirnidhI.NrakR^iNodusriyANAm || 10.68.6
bR^ihaspatiramata hi tyadAsAM nAma svarINAM sadane guhA yat |ANDeva bhittvA shakunasya garbhamudusriyAH parvatasya tmanAjat || 10.68.7
ashnApinaddhaM madhu paryapashyanmatsyaM na dIna udani kShiyantam |niShTajjabhAra chamasaM na vR^ikShAdbR^ihaspatirviraveNA vikR^itya || 10.68.8
soShAmavindatsa svaH so agniM so arkeNa vi babAdhe tamAMsi |bR^ihaspatirgovapuSho valasya nirmajjAnaM na parvaNo jabhAra || 10.68.9
himeva parNA muShitA vanAni bR^ihaspatinAkR^ipayadvalo gAH |anAnukR^ityamapunashchakAra yAtsUryAmAsA mitha uchcharAtaH || 10.68.10
abhi shyAvaM na kR^ishanebhirashvaM nakShatrebhiH pitaro dyAmapiMshan |rAtryAM tamo adadhurjyotirahanbR^ihaspatirbhinadadriM vidadgAH || 10.68.11
idamakarma namo abhriyAya yaH pUrvIranvAnonavIti |bR^ihaspatiH sa hi gobhiH so ashvaiH sa vIrebhiH sa nR^ibhirno vayo dhAt || 10.68.12

bhadrA agnervadhryashvasya saMdR^isho vAmI praNItiH suraNA upetayaH |yadIM sumitrA visho agra indhate ghR^itenAhuto jarate davidyutat || 10.69.1
ghR^itamagnervadhryashvasya vardhanaM ghR^itamannaM ghR^itamvasya medanam |ghR^itenAhuta urviyA vi paprathe sUrya iva rochate sarpirAsutiH || 10.69.2
yatte manuryadanIkaM sumitraH samIdhe agne tadidaM navIyaH |sa revachChocha sa giro juShasva sa vAjaM darShi sa iha shravo dhAH || 10.69.3
yaM tvA pUrvamILito vadhryashvaH samIdhe agne sa idaM juShasva |sa naH stipA uta bhavA tanUpA dAtraM rakShasva yadidaM te asme || 10.69.4
bhavA dyumnI vAdhryashvota gopA mA tvA tArIdabhimAtirjanAnAm |shUra iva dhR^iShNushchyavanaH sumitraH pra nu vochaM vAdhryashvasya nAma || 10.69.5
samajryA parvatyA vasUni dAsA vR^itrANyAryA jigetha |shUra iva dhR^iShNushchyavano janAnAM tvamagne pR^itanAyU.Nrabhi ShyAH || 10.69.6
dIrghatanturbR^ihadukShAyamagniH sahasrastarIH shatanItha R^ibhvA |dyumAndyumatsu nR^ibhirmR^ijyamAnaH sumitreShu dIdayo devayatsu || 10.69.7
tve dhenuH sudughA jAtavedo.asashchateva samanA sabardhuk |tvaM nR^ibhirdakShiNAvadbhiragne sumitrebhiridhyase devayadbhiH || 10.69.8
devAshchitte amR^itA jAtavedo mahimAnaM vAdhryashva pra vochan |yatsampR^ichChaM mAnuShIrvisha AyantvaM nR^ibhirajayastvAvR^idhebhiH || 10.69.9
piteva putramabibharupasthe tvAmagne vadhryashvaH saparyan |juShANo asya samidhaM yaviShThota pUrvA.N avanorvrAdhatashchit || 10.69.10
shashvadagnirvadhryashvasya shatrUnnR^ibhirjigAya sutasomavadbhiH |samanaM chidadahashchitrabhAno.ava vrAdhantamabhinadvR^idhashchit || 10.69.11
ayamagnirvadhryashvasya vR^itrahA sanakAtpreddho namasopavAkyaH |sa no ajAmI.Nruta vA vijAmInabhi tiShTha shardhato vAdhryashva || 10.69.12

imAM me agne samidhaM juShasveLaspade prati haryA ghR^itAchIm |varShmanpR^ithivyAH sudinatve ahnAmUrdhvo bhava sukrato devayajyA || 10.70.1
A devAnAmagrayAveha yAtu narAshaMso vishvarUpebhirashvaiH |R^itasya pathA namasA miyedho devebhyo devatamaH suShUdat || 10.70.2

devAnAM nu vayaM jAnA pra vochAma vipanyayA |uktheShu shasyamAneShu yaH pashyAduttare yuge || 10.72.1

vasUnAM vA charkR^iSha iyakShandhiyA vA yaj~nairvA rodasyoH |arvanto vA ye rayimantaH sAtau vanuM vA ye sushruNaM sushruto dhuH || 10.74.1

A va R^i~njasa UrjAM vyuShTiShvindraM maruto rodasI anaktana |ubhe yathA no ahanI sachAbhuvA sadaHsado varivasyAta udbhidA || 10.76.1

tvayA manyo sarathamArujanto harShamANAso dhR^iShitA marutvaH |tigmeShava AyudhA saMshishAnA abhi pra yantu naro agnirUpAH || 10.84.1

rakShohaNaM vAjinamA jigharmi mitraM prathiShThamupa yAmi sharma |shishAno agniH kratubhiH samiddhaH sa no divA sa riShaH pAtu naktam || 10.87.1

kadA vaso stotraM haryata Ava shmashA rudhadvAH |dIrghaM sutaM vAtApyAya || 10.105.1

AvirabhUnmahi mAghonameShAM vishvaM jIvaM tamaso niramochi |mahi jyotiH pitR^ibhirdattamAgAduruH panthA dakShiNAyA adarshi || 10.107.1

kIdR^i~N~NindraH sarame kA dR^ishIkA yasyedaM dUtIrasaraH parAkAt |A cha gachChAnmitramenA dadhAmAthA gavAM gopatirno bhavAti || 10.108.3
nAhaM taM veda dabhyaM dabhatsa yasyedaM dUtIrasaraM parAkAt |na taM gUhanti sravato gabhIrA hatA indreNa paNayaH shayadhve || 10.108.4
imA gAvaH sarame yA aichChaH pari divo antAnsubhage patantI |kasta enA ava sR^ijAdayudhvyutAsmAkamAyudhA santi tigmA || 10.108.5
asenyA vaH paNayo vachAMsyaniShavyAstanvaH santu pApIH |adhR^iShTo va etavA astu panthA bR^ihaspatirva ubhayA na mR^iLAt || 10.108.6
ayaM nidhiH sarame adribudhno gobhirashvebhirvasubhirnyR^iShTaH |rakShanti taM paNayo ye sugopA reku padamalakamA jagantha || 10.108.7
eha gamannR^iShayaH somashitA ayAsyo a~Ngiraso navagvAH |ta etamUrvaM vi bhajanta gonAmathaitadvachaH paNayo vamannit || 10.108.8
evA cha tvaM sarama Ajagantha prabAdhitA sahasA daivyena |svasAraM tvA kR^iNavai mA punargA apa te gavAM subhage bhajAma || 10.108.9
nAhaM veda bhrAtR^itvaM no svasR^itvamindro vidura~Ngirasashcha ghorAH |gokAmA me achChadayanyadAyamapAta ita paNayo varIyaH || 10.108.10
dUramita paNayo varIya udgAvo yantu minatIrR^itena |bR^ihaspatiryA avindannigULhAH somo grAvANa R^iShayashcha viprAH || 10.108.11

te.avadanprathamA brahmakilbiShe.akUpAraH salilo mAtarishvA |vILuharAstapa ugro mayobhUrApo devIH prathamajA R^itena || 10.109.1
somo rAjA prathamo brahmajAyAM punaH prAyachChadahR^iNIyamAnaH |anvartitA varuNo mitra AsIdagnirhotA hastagR^ihyA ninAya || 10.109.2
hastenaiva grAhya AdhirasyA brahmajAyeyamiti chedavochan |na dUtAya prahye tastha eShA tathA rAShTraM gupitaM kShatriyasya || 10.109.3
devA etasyAmavadanta pUrve saptaR^iShayastapase ye niSheduH |bhImA jAyA brAhmaNasyopanItA durdhAM dadhAti parame vyoman || 10.109.4
brahmachArI charati veviShadviShaH sa devAnAM bhavatyekama~Ngam |tena jAyAmanvavindadbR^ihaspatiH somena nItAM juhvaM na devAH || 10.109.5
punarvai devA adaduH punarmanuShyA uta |rAjAnaH satyaM kR^iNvAnA brahmajAyAM punardaduH || 10.109.6
punardAya brahmajAyAM kR^itvI devairnikilbiSham |UrjaM pR^ithivyA bhaktvAyorugAyamupAsate || 10.109.7

samiddho adya manuSho duroNe devo devAnyajasi jAtavedaH |A cha vaha mitramahashchikitvAntvaM dUtaH kavirasi prachetAH || 10.110.1
tanUnapAtpatha R^itasya yAnAnmadhvA sama~njansvadayA sujihva |manmAni dhIbhiruta yaj~namR^indhandevatrA cha kR^iNuhyadhvaraM naH || 10.110.2
AjuhvAna IDyo vandyashchA yAhyagne vasubhiH sajoShAH |tvaM devAnAmasi yahva hotA sa enAnyakShIShito yajIyAn || 10.110.3
prAchInaM barhiH pradishA pR^ithivyA vastorasyA vR^ijyate agre ahnAm |vyu prathate vitaraM varIyo devebhyo aditaye syonam || 10.110.4
vyachasvatIrurviyA vi shrayantAM patibhyo na janayaH shumbhamAnAH |devIrdvAro bR^ihatIrvishvaminvA devebhyo bhavata suprAyaNAH || 10.110.5
A suShvayantI yajate upAke uShAsAnaktA sadatAM ni yonau |divye yoShaNe bR^ihatI surukme adhi shriyaM shukrapishaM dadhAne || 10.110.6
daivyA hotArA prathamA suvAchA mimAnA yaj~naM manuSho yajadhyai |prachodayantA vidatheShu kArU prAchInaM jyotiH pradishA dishantA || 10.110.7
A no yaj~naM bhAratI tUyametviLA manuShvadiha chetayantI |tisro devIrbarhiredaM syonaM sarasvatI svapasaH sadantu || 10.110.8
ya ime dyAvApR^ithivI janitrI rUpairapiMshadbhuvanAni vishvA |tamadya hotariShito yajIyAndevaM tvaShTAramiha yakShi vidvAn || 10.110.9
upAvasR^ija tmanyA sama~njandevAnAM pAtha R^ituthA havIMShi |vanaspatiH shamitA devo agniH svadantu havyaM madhunA ghR^itena || 10.110.10
sadyo jAto vyamimIta yaj~namagnirdevAnAmabhavatpurogAH |asya hotuH pradishyR^itasya vAchi svAhAkR^itaM haviradantu devAH || 10.110.11

manIShiNaH pra bharadhvaM manIShAM yathAyathA matayaH santi nR^iNAm |indraM satyairerayAmA kR^itebhiH sa hi vIro girvaNasyurvidAnaH || 10.111.1
R^itasya hi sadaso dhItiradyautsaM gArShTeyo vR^iShabho gobhirAnaT |udatiShThattaviSheNA raveNa mahAnti chitsaM vivyAchA rajAMsi || 10.111.2
indraH kila shrutyA asya veda sa hi jiShNuH pathikR^itsUryAya |AnmenAM kR^iNvannachyuto bhuvadgoH patirdivaH sanajA apratItaH || 10.111.3
indro mahnA mahato arNavasya vratAminAda~NgirobhirgR^iNAnaH |purUNi chinni tatAnA rajAMsi dAdhAra yo dharuNaM satyatAtA || 10.111.4
indro divaH pratimAnaM pR^ithivyA vishvA veda savanA hanti shuShNam |mahIM chiddyAmAtanotsUryeNa chAskambha chitkambhanena skabhIyAn || 10.111.5
vajreNa hi vR^itrahA vR^itramastaradevasya shUshuvAnasya mAyAH |vi dhR^iShNo atra dhR^iShatA jaghanthAthAbhavo maghavanbAhvojAH || 10.111.6
sachanta yaduShasaH sUryeNa chitrAmasya ketavo rAmavindan |A yannakShatraM dadR^ishe divo na punaryato nakiraddhA nu veda || 10.111.7
dUraM kila prathamA jagmurAsAmindrasya yAH prasave sasrurApaH |kva svidagraM kva budhna AsAmApo madhyaM kva vo nUnamantaH || 10.111.8
sR^ijaH sindhU.NrahinA jagrasAnA.N AdidetAH pra vivijre javena |mumukShamANA uta yA mumuchre.adhedetA na ramante nitiktAH || 10.111.9
sadhrIchIH sindhumushatIrivAyansanAjjAra AritaH pUrbhidAsAm |astamA te pArthivA vasUnyasme jagmuH sUnR^itA indra pUrvIH || 10.111.10

indra piba pratikAmaM sutasya prAtaHsAvastava hi pUrvapItiH |harShasva hantave shUra shatrUnukthebhiShTe vIryA pra bravAma || 10.112.1
yaste ratho manaso javIyAnendra tena somapeyAya yAhi |tUyamA te harayaH pra dravantu yebhiryAsi vR^iShabhirmandamAnaH || 10.112.2
haritvatA varchasA sUryasya shreShThai rUpaistanvaM sparshayasva |asmAbhirindra sakhibhirhuvAnaH sadhrIchIno mAdayasvA niShadya || 10.112.3
yasya tyatte mahimAnaM madeShvime mahI rodasI nAviviktAm |tadoka A haribhirindra yuktaiH priyebhiryAhi priyamannamachCha || 10.112.4
yasya shashvatpapivA.N indra shatrUnanAnukR^ityA raNyA chakartha |sa te puraMdhiM taviShImiyarti sa te madAya suta indra somaH || 10.112.5
idaM te pAtraM sanavittamindra pibA somamenA shatakrato |pUrNa AhAvo madirasya madhvo yaM vishva idabhiharyanti devAH || 10.112.6
vi hi tvAmindra purudhA janAso hitaprayaso vR^iShabha hvayante |asmAkaM te madhumattamAnImA bhuvansavanA teShu harya || 10.112.7
pra ta indra pUrvyANi pra nUnaM vIryA vochaM prathamA kR^itAni |satInamanyurashrathAyo adriM suvedanAmakR^iNorbrahmaNe gAm || 10.112.8
ni Shu sIda gaNapate gaNeShu tvAmAhurvipratamaM kavInAm |na R^ite tvatkriyate kiM chanAre mahAmarkaM maghava~nchitramarcha || 10.112.9
abhikhyA no maghavannAdhamAnAnsakhe bodhi vasupate sakhInAm |raNaM kR^idhi raNakR^itsatyashuShmAbhakte chidA bhajA rAye asmAn || 10.112.10

tamasya dyAvApR^ithivI sachetasA vishvebhirdevairanu shuShmamAvatAm |yadaitkR^iNvAno mahimAnamindriyaM pItvI somasya kratumA.N avardhata || 10.113.1
tamasya viShNurmahimAnamojasAMshuM dadhanvAnmadhuno vi rapshate |devebhirindro maghavA sayAvabhirvR^itraM jaghanvA.N abhavadvareNyaH || 10.113.2
vR^itreNa yadahinA bibhradAyudhA samasthithA yudhaye shaMsamAvide |vishve te atra marutaH saha tmanAvardhannugra mahimAnamindriyam || 10.113.3
jaj~nAna eva vyabAdhata spR^idhaH prApashyadvIro abhi pauMsyaM raNam |avR^ishchadadrimava sasyadaH sR^ijadastabhnAnnAkaM svapasyayA pR^ithum || 10.113.4
AdindraH satrA taviShIrapatyata varIyo dyAvApR^ithivI abAdhata |avAbharaddhR^iShito vajramAyasaM shevaM mitrAya varuNAya dAshuShe || 10.113.5
indrasyAtra taviShIbhyo virapshina R^ighAyato araMhayanta manyave |vR^itraM yadugro vyavR^ishchadojasApo bibhrataM tamasA parIvR^itam || 10.113.6
yA vIryANi prathamAni kartvA mahitvebhiryatamAnau samIyatuH |dhvAntaM tamo.ava dadhvase hata indro mahnA pUrvahUtAvapatyata || 10.113.7
vishve devAso adha vR^iShNyAni te.avardhayansomavatyA vachasyayA |raddhaM vR^itramahimindrasya hanmanAgnirna jambhaistR^iShvannamAvayat || 10.113.8
bhUri dakShebhirvachanebhirR^ikvabhiH sakhyebhiH sakhyAni pra vochata |indro dhuniM cha chumuriM cha dambhaya~nChraddhAmanasyA shR^iNute dabhItaye || 10.113.9
tvaM purUNyA bharA svashvyA yebhirmaMsai nivachanAni shaMsan |sugebhirvishvA duritA tarema vido Shu Na urviyA gAdhamadya || 10.113.10

gharmA samantA trivR^itaM vyApatustayorjuShTiM mAtarishvA jagAma |divaspayo didhiShANA aveShanvidurdevAH sahasAmAnamarkam || 10.114.1
tisro deShTrAya nirR^itIrupAsate dIrghashruto vi hi jAnanti vahnayaH |tAsAM ni chikyuH kavayo nidAnaM pareShu yA guhyeShu vrateShu || 10.114.2
chatuShkapardA yuvatiH supeshA ghR^itapratIkA vayunAni vaste |tasyAM suparNA vR^iShaNA ni Shedaturyatra devA dadhire bhAgadheyam || 10.114.3
ekaH suparNaH sa samudramA vivesha sa idaM vishvaM bhuvanaM vi chaShTe |taM pAkena manasApashyamantitastaM mAtA reLhi sa u reLhi mAtaram || 10.114.4
suparNaM viprAH kavayo vachobhirekaM santaM bahudhA kalpayanti |ChandAMsi cha dadhato adhvareShu grahAnsomasya mimate dvAdasha || 10.114.5
ShaTtriMshA.Nshcha chaturaH kalpayantashChandAMsi cha dadhata AdvAdasham |yaj~naM vimAya kavayo manISha R^iksAmAbhyAM pra rathaM vartayanti || 10.114.6
chaturdashAnye mahimAno asya taM dhIrA vAchA pra Nayanti sapta |ApnAnaM tIrthaM ka iha pra vochadyena pathA prapibante sutasya || 10.114.7
sahasradhA pa~nchadashAnyukthA yAvaddyAvApR^ithivI tAvadittat |sahasradhA mahimAnaH sahasraM yAvadbrahma viShThitaM tAvatI vAk || 10.114.8
kashChandasAM yogamA veda dhIraH ko dhiShNyAM prati vAchaM papAda |kamR^itvijAmaShTamaM shUramAhurharI indrasya ni chikAya kaH svit || 10.114.9
bhUmyA antaM paryeke charanti rathasya dhUrShu yuktAso asthuH |shramasya dAyaM vi bhajantyebhyo yadA yamo bhavati harmye hitaH || 10.114.10

chitra ichChishostaruNasya vakShatho na yo mAtarAvapyeti dhAtave |anUdhA yadi jIjanadadhA cha nu vavakSha sadyo mahi dUtyaM charan || 10.115.1
agnirha nAma dhAyi dannapastamaH saM yo vanA yuvate bhasmanA datA |abhipramurA juhvA svadhvara ino na prothamAno yavase vR^iShA || 10.115.2
taM vo viM na druShadaM devamandhasa induM prothantaM pravapantamarNavam |AsA vahniM na shochiShA virapshinaM mahivrataM na sarajantamadhvanaH || 10.115.3
vi yasya te jrayasAnasyAjara dhakShorna vAtAH pari santyachyutAH |A raNvAso yuyudhayo na satvanaM tritaM nashanta pra shiShanta iShTaye || 10.115.4
sa idagniH kaNvatamaH kaNvasakhAryaH parasyAntarasya taruShaH |agniH pAtu gR^iNato agniH sUrInagnirdadAtu teShAmavo naH || 10.115.5
vAjintamAya sahyase supitrya tR^iShu chyavAno anu jAtavedase |anudre chidyo dhR^iShatA varaM sate mahintamAya dhanvanedaviShyate || 10.115.6
evAgnirmartaiH saha sUribhirvasuH ShTave sahasaH sUnaro nR^ibhiH |mitrAso na ye sudhitA R^itAyavo dyAvo na dyumnairabhi santi mAnuShAn || 10.115.7
Urjo napAtsahasAvanniti tvopastutasya vandate vR^iShA vAk |tvAM stoShAma tvayA suvIrA drAghIya AyuH prataraM dadhAnAH || 10.115.8
iti tvAgne vR^iShTihavyasya putrA upastutAsa R^iShayo.avochan |tA.Nshcha pAhi gR^iNatashcha sUrInvaShaDvaShaLityUrdhvAso anakShannamo nama ityUrdhvAso anakShan || 10.115.9

pibA somaM mahata indriyAya pibA vR^itrAya hantave shaviShTha |piba rAye shavase hUyamAnaH piba madhvastR^ipadindrA vR^iShasva || 10.116.1
asya piba kShumataH prasthitasyendra somasya varamA sutasya |svastidA manasA mAdayasvArvAchIno revate saubhagAya || 10.116.2
mamattu tvA divyaH soma indra mamattu yaH sUyate pArthiveShu |mamattu yena varivashchakartha mamattu yena niriNAsi shatrUn || 10.116.3
A dvibarhA amino yAtvindro vR^iShA haribhyAM pariShiktamandhaH |gavyA sutasya prabhR^itasya madhvaH satrA khedAmarushahA vR^iShasva || 10.116.4
ni tigmAni bhrAshayanbhrAshyAnyava sthirA tanuhi yAtujUnAm |ugrAya te saho balaM dadAmi pratItyA shatrUnvigadeShu vR^ishcha || 10.116.5
vyarya indra tanuhi shravAMsyojaH sthireva dhanvano.abhimAtIH |asmadryagvAvR^idhAnaH sahobhiranibhR^iShTastanvaM vAvR^idhasva || 10.116.6
idaM havirmaghavantubhyaM rAtaM prati samrALahR^iNAno gR^ibhAya |tubhyaM suto maghavantubhyaM pakvo.addhIndra piba cha prasthitasya || 10.116.7
addhIdindra prasthitemA havIMShi chano dadhiShva pachatota somam |prayasvantaH prati haryAmasi tvA satyAH santu yajamAnasya kAmAH || 10.116.8
prendrAgnibhyAM suvachasyAmiyarmi sindhAviva prerayaM nAvamarkaiH |ayA iva pari charanti devA ye asmabhyaM dhanadA udbhidashcha || 10.116.9

na vA u devAH kShudhamidvadhaM dadurutAshitamupa gachChanti mR^ityavaH |uto rayiH pR^iNato nopa dasyatyutApR^iNanmarDitAraM na vindate || 10.117.1
ya AdhrAya chakamAnAya pitvo.annavAnsanraphitAyopajagmuShe |sthiraM manaH kR^iNute sevate puroto chitsa marDitAraM na vindate || 10.117.2
sa idbhojo yo gR^ihave dadAtyannakAmAya charate kR^ishAya |aramasmai bhavati yAmahUtA utAparIShu kR^iNute sakhAyam || 10.117.3
na sa sakhA yo na dadAti sakhye sachAbhuve sachamAnAya pitvaH |apAsmAtpreyAnna tadoko asti pR^iNantamanyamaraNaM chidichChet || 10.117.4
pR^iNIyAdinnAdhamAnAya tavyAndrAghIyAMsamanu pashyeta panthAm |o hi vartante rathyeva chakrAnyamanyamupa tiShThanta rAyaH || 10.117.5
moghamannaM vindate aprachetAH satyaM bravImi vadha itsa tasya |nAryamaNaM puShyati no sakhAyaM kevalAgho bhavati kevalAdI || 10.117.6
kR^iShannitphAla AshitaM kR^iNoti yannadhvAnamapa vR^i~Nkte charitraiH |vadanbrahmAvadato vanIyAnpR^iNannApirapR^iNantamabhi ShyAt || 10.117.7
ekapAdbhUyo dvipado vi chakrame dvipAttripAdamabhyeti pashchAt |chatuShpAdeti dvipadAmabhisvare sampashyanpa~NktIrupatiShThamAnaH || 10.117.8
samau chiddhastau na samaM viviShTaH sammAtarA chinna samaM duhAte |yamayoshchinna samA vIryANi j~nAtI chitsantau na samaM pR^iNItaH || 10.117.9

agne haMsi nyatriNaM dIdyanmartyeShvA |sve kShaye shuchivrata || 10.118.1
uttiShThasi svAhuto ghR^itAni prati modase |yattvA sruchaH samasthiran || 10.118.2
sa Ahuto vi rochate.agnirILenyo girA |sruchA pratIkamajyate || 10.118.3
ghR^itenAgniH samajyate madhupratIka AhutaH |rochamAno vibhAvasuH || 10.118.4
jaramANaH samidhyase devebhyo havyavAhana |taM tvA havanta martyAH || 10.118.5
taM martA amartyaM ghR^itenAgniM saparyata |adAbhyaM gR^ihapatim || 10.118.6
adAbhyena shochiShAgne rakShastvaM daha |gopA R^itasya dIdihi || 10.118.7
