taM tvA gIrbhirurukShayA havyavAhaM samIdhire |yajiShThaM mAnuShe jane || 10.118.9

iti vA iti me mano gAmashvaM sanuyAmiti |kuvitsomasyApAmiti || 10.119.1
pra vAtA iva dodhata unmA pItA ayaMsata |kuvitsomasyApAmiti || 10.119.2
unmA pItA ayaMsata rathamashvA ivAshavaH |kuvitsomasyApAmiti || 10.119.3
upa mA matirasthita vAshrA putramiva priyam |kuvitsomasyApAmiti || 10.119.4
ahaM taShTeva vandhuraM paryachAmi hR^idA matim |kuvitsomasyApAmiti || 10.119.5
nahi me akShipachchanAchChAntsuH pa~ncha kR^iShTayaH |kuvitsomasyApAmiti || 10.119.6
nahi me rodasI ubhe anyaM pakShaM chana prati |kuvitsomasyApAmiti || 10.119.7
abhi dyAM mahinA bhuvamabhImAM pR^ithivIM mahIm |kuvitsomasyApAmiti || 10.119.8
hantAhaM pR^ithivImimAM ni dadhAnIha veha vA |kuvitsomasyApAmiti || 10.119.9
oShamitpR^ithivImahaM ja~NghanAnIha veha vA |kuvitsomasyApAmiti || 10.119.10
divi me anyaH pakSho.adho anyamachIkR^iSham |kuvitsomasyApAmiti || 10.119.11
ahamasmi mahAmaho.abhinabhyamudIShitaH |kuvitsomasyApAmiti || 10.119.12
gR^iho yAmyaraMkR^ito devebhyo havyavAhanaH |kuvitsomasyApAmiti || 10.119.13

tadidAsa bhuvaneShu jyeShThaM yato jaj~na ugrastveShanR^imNaH |sadyo jaj~nAno ni riNAti shatrUnanu yaM vishve madantyUmAH || 10.120.1
vAvR^idhAnaH shavasA bhUryojAH shatrurdAsAya bhiyasaM dadhAti |avyanachcha vyanachcha sasni saM te navanta prabhR^itA madeShu || 10.120.2
tve kratumapi vR^i~njanti vishve dviryadete trirbhavantyUmAH |svAdoH svAdIyaH svAdunA sR^ijA samadaH su madhu madhunAbhi yodhIH || 10.120.3
iti chiddhi tvA dhanA jayantaM mademade anumadanti viprAH |ojIyo dhR^iShNo sthiramA tanuShva mA tvA dabhanyAtudhAnA durevAH || 10.120.4
tvayA vayaM shAshadmahe raNeShu prapashyanto yudhenyAni bhUri |chodayAmi ta AyudhA vachobhiH saM te shishAmi brahmaNA vayAMsi || 10.120.5
stuSheyyaM puruvarpasamR^ibhvaminatamamAptyamAptyAnAm |A darShate shavasA sapta dAnUnpra sAkShate pratimAnAni bhUri || 10.120.6
ni taddadhiShe.avaraM paraM cha yasminnAvithAvasA duroNe |A mAtarA sthApayase jigatnU ata inoShi karvarA purUNi || 10.120.7
imA brahma bR^ihaddivo vivaktIndrAya shUShamagriyaH svarShAH |maho gotrasya kShayati svarAjo durashcha vishvA avR^iNodapa svAH || 10.120.8
evA mahAnbR^ihaddivo atharvAvochatsvAM tanvamindrameva |svasAro mAtaribhvarIrariprA hinvanti cha shavasA vardhayanti cha || 10.120.9

hiraNyagarbhaH samavartatAgre bhUtasya jAtaH patireka AsIt |sa dAdhAra pR^ithivIM dyAmutemAM kasmai devAya haviShA vidhema || 10.121.1
ya AtmadA baladA yasya vishva upAsate prashiShaM yasya devAH |yasya ChAyAmR^itaM yasya mR^ityuH kasmai devAya haviShA vidhema || 10.121.2
yaH prANato nimiShato mahitvaika idrAjA jagato babhUva |ya Ishe asya dvipadashchatuShpadaH kasmai devAya haviShA vidhema || 10.121.3
yasyeme himavanto mahitvA yasya samudraM rasayA sahAhuH |yasyemAH pradisho yasya bAhU kasmai devAya haviShA vidhema || 10.121.4
yena dyaurugrA pR^ithivI cha dR^iLhA yena svaH stabhitaM yena nAkaH |yo antarikShe rajaso vimAnaH kasmai devAya haviShA vidhema || 10.121.5

ajaiShmAdyAsanAma chAbhUmAnAgaso vayam |jAgratsvapnaH saMkalpaH pApo yaM dviShmastaM sa R^ichChatu yo no dveShTi tamR^ichChatu || 10.164.5

devAH kapota iShito yadichChandUto nirR^ityA idamAjagAma |tasmA archAma kR^iNavAma niShkR^itiM shaM no astu dvipade shaM chatuShpade || 10.165.1
shivaH kapota iShito no astvanAgA devAH shakuno gR^iheShu |agnirhi vipro juShatAM havirnaH pari hetiH pakShiNI no vR^iNaktu || 10.165.2
hetiH pakShiNI na dabhAtyasmAnAShTryAM padaM kR^iNute agnidhAne |shaM no gobhyashcha puruShebhyashchAstu mA no hiMsIdiha devAH kapotaH || 10.165.3
yadulUko vadati moghametadyatkapotaH padamagnau kR^iNoti |yasya dUtaH prahita eSha etattasmai yamAya namo astu mR^ityave || 10.165.4
R^ichA kapotaM nudata praNodamiShaM madantaH pari gAM nayadhvam |saMyopayanto duritAni vishvA hitvA na UrjaM pra patAtpatiShThaH || 10.165.5

R^iShabhaM mA samAnAnAM sapatnAnAM viShAsahim |hantAraM shatrUNAM kR^idhi virAjaM gopatiM gavAm || 10.166.1
ahamasmi sapatnahendra ivAriShTo akShataH |adhaH sapatnA me padorime sarve abhiShThitAH || 10.166.2
atraiva vo.api nahyAmyubhe ArtnI iva jyayA |vAchaspate ni ShedhemAnyathA madadharaM vadAn || 10.166.3
abhibhUrahamAgamaM vishvakarmeNa dhAmnA |A vashchittamA vo vratamA vo.ahaM samitiM dade || 10.166.4
yogakShemaM va AdAyAhaM bhUyAsamuttama A vo mUrdhAnamakramIm |adhaspadAnma udvadata maNDUkA ivodakAnmaNDUkA udakAdiva || 10.166.5

tubhyedamindra pari Shichyate madhu tvaM sutasya kalashasya rAjasi |tvaM rayiM puruvIrAmu naskR^idhi tvaM tapaH paritapyAjayaH svaH || 10.167.1
svarjitaM mahi mandAnamandhaso havAmahe pari shakraM sutA.N upa |imaM no yaj~namiha bodhyA gahi spR^idho jayantaM maghavAnamImahe || 10.167.2
somasya rAj~no varuNasya dharmaNi bR^ihaspateranumatyA u sharmaNi |tavAhamadya maghavannupastutau dhAtarvidhAtaH kalashA.N abhakShayam || 10.167.3
prasUto bhakShamakaraM charAvapi stomaM chemaM prathamaH sUrirunmR^ije |sute sAtena yadyAgamaM vAM prati vishvAmitrajamadagnI dame || 10.167.4

vAtasya nu mahimAnaM rathasya rujanneti stanayannasya ghoShaH |divispR^igyAtyaruNAni kR^iNvannuto eti pR^ithivyA reNumasyan || 10.168.1
saM prerate anu vAtasya viShThA ainaM gachChanti samanaM na yoShAH |tAbhiH sayuksarathaM deva Iyate.asya vishvasya bhuvanasya rAjA || 10.168.2
antarikShe pathibhirIyamAno na ni vishate katamachchanAhaH |apAM sakhA prathamajA R^itAvA kva svijjAtaH kuta A babhUva || 10.168.3
AtmA devAnAM bhuvanasya garbho yathAvashaM charati deva eShaH |ghoShA idasya shR^iNvire na rUpaM tasmai vAtAya haviShA vidhema || 10.168.4

mayobhUrvAto abhi vAtUsrA UrjasvatIroShadhIrA rishantAm |pIvasvatIrjIvadhanyAH pibantvavasAya padvate rudra mR^iLa || 10.169.1
yAH sarUpA virUpA ekarUpA yAsAmagniriShTyA nAmAni veda |yA a~Ngirasastapaseha chakrustAbhyaH parjanya mahi sharma yachCha || 10.169.2
yA deveShu tanvamairayanta yAsAM somo vishvA rUpANi veda |tA asmabhyaM payasA pinvamAnAH prajAvatIrindra goShThe rirIhi || 10.169.3
prajApatirmahyametA rarANo vishvairdevaiH pitR^ibhiH saMvidAnaH |shivAH satIrupa no goShThamAkastAsAM vayaM prajayA saM sadema || 10.169.4

vibhrADbR^ihatpibatu somyaM madhvAyurdadhadyaj~napatAvavihrutam |vAtajUto yo abhirakShati tmanA prajAH pupoSha purudhA vi rAjati || 10.170.1
vibhrADbR^ihatsubhR^itaM vAjasAtamaM dharmandivo dharuNe satyamarpitam |amitrahA vR^itrahA dasyuhantamaM jyotirjaj~ne asurahA sapatnahA || 10.170.2
idaM shreShThaM jyotiShAM jyotiruttamaM vishvajiddhanajiduchyate bR^ihat |vishvabhrADbhrAjo mahi sUryo dR^isha uru paprathe saha ojo achyutam || 10.170.3
vibhrAja~njyotiShA svaragachCho rochanaM divaH |yenemA vishvA bhuvanAnyAbhR^itA vishvakarmaNA vishvadevyAvatA || 10.170.4

tvaM tyamiTato rathamindra prAvaH sutAvataH |ashR^iNoH somino havam || 10.171.1
tvaM makhasya dodhataH shiro.ava tvacho bharaH |agachChaH somino gR^iham || 10.171.2
tvaM tyamindra martyamAstrabudhnAya venyam |muhuH shrathnA manasyave || 10.171.3
tvaM tyamindra sUryaM pashchA santaM puraskR^idhi |devAnAM chittiro vasham || 10.171.4

A yAhi vanasA saha gAvaH sachanta vartaniM yadUdhabhiH || 10.172.1
A yAhi vasvyA dhiyA maMhiShTho jArayanmakhaH sudAnubhiH || 10.172.2
pitubhR^ito na tantumitsudAnavaH prati dadhmo yajAmasi || 10.172.3
uShA apa svasustamaH saM vartayati vartaniM sujAtatA || 10.172.4

A tvAhArShamantaredhi dhruvastiShThAvichAchaliH |vishastvA sarvA vA~nChantu mA tvadrAShTramadhi bhrashat || 10.173.1
ihaivaidhi mApa chyoShThAH parvata ivAvichAchaliH |indra iveha dhruvastiShTheha rAShTramu dhAraya || 10.173.2
imamindro adIdharaddhruvaM dhruveNa haviShA |tasmai somo adhi bravattasmA u brahmaNaspatiH || 10.173.3
dhruvA dyaurdhruvA pR^ithivI dhruvAsaH parvatA ime |dhruvaM vishvamidaM jagaddhruvo rAjA vishAmayam || 10.173.4
dhruvaM te rAjA varuNo dhruvaM devo bR^ihaspatiH |dhruvaM ta indrashchAgnishcha rAShTraM dhArayatAM dhruvam || 10.173.5
dhruvaM dhruveNa haviShAbhi somaM mR^ishAmasi |atho ta indraH kevalIrvisho balihR^itaskarat || 10.173.6

abhIvartena haviShA yenendro abhivAvR^ite |tenAsmAnbrahmaNaspate.abhi rAShTrAya vartaya || 10.174.1
abhivR^itya sapatnAnabhi yA no arAtayaH |abhi pR^itanyantaM tiShThAbhi yo na irasyati || 10.174.2
abhi tvA devaH savitAbhi somo avIvR^itat |abhi tvA vishvA bhUtAnyabhIvarto yathAsasi || 10.174.3
yenendro haviShA kR^itvyabhavaddyumnyuttamaH |idaM tadakri devA asapatnaH kilAbhuvam || 10.174.4
asapatnaH sapatnahAbhirAShTro viShAsahiH |yathAhameShAM bhUtAnAM virAjAni janasya cha || 10.174.5

pra vo grAvANaH savitA devaH suvatu dharmaNA |dhUrShu yujyadhvaM sunuta || 10.175.1
grAvANo apa duchChunAmapa sedhata durmatim |usrAH kartana bheShajam || 10.175.2
grAvANa upareShvA mahIyante sajoShasaH |vR^iShNe dadhato vR^iShNyam || 10.175.3
grAvANaH savitA nu vo devaH suvatu dharmaNA |yajamAnAya sunvate || 10.175.4

pra sUnava R^ibhUNAM bR^ihannavanta vR^ijanA |kShAmA ye vishvadhAyaso.ashnandhenuM na mAtaram || 10.176.1
pra devaM devyA dhiyA bharatA jAtavedasam |havyA no vakShadAnuShak || 10.176.2
ayamu Shya pra devayurhotA yaj~nAya nIyate |ratho na yorabhIvR^ito ghR^iNIvA~nchetati tmanA || 10.176.3
ayamagniruruShyatyamR^itAdiva janmanaH |sahasashchitsahIyAndevo jIvAtave kR^itaH || 10.176.4

pataMgamaktamasurasya mAyayA hR^idA pashyanti manasA vipashchitaH |samudre antaH kavayo vi chakShate marIchInAM padamichChanti vedhasaH || 10.177.1
pataMgo vAchaM manasA bibharti tAM gandharvo.avadadgarbhe antaH |tAM dyotamAnAM svaryaM manIShAmR^itasya pade kavayo ni pAnti || 10.177.2
apashyaM gopAmanipadyamAnamA cha parA cha pathibhishcharantam |sa sadhrIchIH sa viShUchIrvasAna A varIvarti bhuvaneShvantaH || 10.177.3

tyamU Shu vAjinaM devajUtaM sahAvAnaM tarutAraM rathAnAm |ariShTanemiM pR^itanAjamAshuM svastaye tArkShyamihA huvema || 10.178.1
indrasyeva rAtimAjohuvAnAH svastaye nAvamivA ruhema |urvI na pR^ithvI bahule gabhIre mA vAmetau mA paretau riShAma || 10.178.2
sadyashchidyaH shavasA pa~ncha kR^iShTIH sUrya iva jyotiShApastatAna |sahasrasAH shatasA asya raMhirna smA varante yuvatiM na sharyAm || 10.178.3

uttiShThatAva pashyatendrasya bhAgamR^itviyam |yadi shrAto juhotana yadyashrAto mamattana || 10.179.1
shrAtaM haviro Shvindra pra yAhi jagAma sUro adhvano vimadhyam |pari tvAsate nidhibhiH sakhAyaH kulapA na vrAjapatiM charantam || 10.179.2
shrAtaM manya Udhani shrAtamagnau sushrAtaM manye tadR^itaM navIyaH |mAdhyaMdinasya savanasya dadhnaH pibendra vajrinpurukR^ijjuShANaH || 10.179.3

pra sasAhiShe puruhUta shatrU~njyeShThaste shuShma iha rAtirastu |indrA bhara dakShiNenA vasUni patiH sindhUnAmasi revatInAm || 10.180.1
mR^igo na bhImaH kucharo giriShThAH parAvata A jaganthA parasyAH |sR^ikaM saMshAya pavimindra tigmaM vi shatrUntALhi vi mR^idho nudasva || 10.180.2
indra kShatramabhi vAmamojo.ajAyathA vR^iShabha charShaNInAm |apAnudo janamamitrayantamuruM devebhyo akR^iNoru lokam || 10.180.3

prathashcha yasya saprathashcha nAmAnuShTubhasya haviSho haviryat |dhAturdyutAnAtsavitushcha viShNo rathaMtaramA jabhArA vasiShThaH || 10.181.1
avindante atihitaM yadAsIdyaj~nasya dhAma paramaM guhA yat |dhAturdyutAnAtsavitushcha viShNorbharadvAjo bR^ihadA chakre agneH || 10.181.2
te.avindanmanasA dIdhyAnA yajuH ShkannaM prathamaM devayAnam |dhAturdyutAnAtsavitushcha viShNorA sUryAdabharangharmamete || 10.181.3

bR^ihaspatirnayatu durgahA tiraH punarneShadaghashaMsAya manma |kShipadashastimapa durmatiM hannathA karadyajamAnAya shaM yoH || 10.182.1
narAshaMso no.avatu prayAje shaM no astvanuyAjo haveShu |kShipadashastimapa durmatiM hannathA karadyajamAnAya shaM yoH || 10.182.2
tapurmUrdhA tapatu rakShaso ye brahmadviShaH sharave hantavA u |kShipadashastimapa durmatiM hannathA karadyajamAnAya shaM yoH || 10.182.3

apashyaM tvA manasA chekitAnaM tapaso jAtaM tapaso vibhUtam |iha prajAmiha rayiM rarANaH pra jAyasva prajayA putrakAma || 10.183.1
apashyaM tvA manasA dIdhyAnAM svAyAM tanU R^itvye nAdhamAnAm |upa mAmuchchA yuvatirbabhUyAH pra jAyasva prajayA putrakAme || 10.183.2
ahaM garbhamadadhAmoShadhIShvahaM vishveShu bhuvaneShvantaH |ahaM prajA ajanayaM pR^ithivyAmahaM janibhyo aparIShu putrAn || 10.183.3

viShNuryoniM kalpayatu tvaShTA rUpANi piMshatu |A si~nchatu prajApatirdhAtA garbhaM dadhAtu te || 10.184.1
garbhaM dhehi sinIvAli garbhaM dhehi sarasvati |garbhaM te ashvinau devAvA dhattAM puShkarasrajA || 10.184.2
hiraNyayI araNI yaM nirmanthato ashvinA |taM te garbhaM havAmahe dashame mAsi sUtave || 10.184.3

mahi trINAmavo.astu dyukShaM mitrasyAryamNaH |durAdharShaM varuNasya || 10.185.1
nahi teShAmamA chana nAdhvasu vAraNeShu |Ishe ripuraghashaMsaH || 10.185.2
yasmai putrAso aditeH pra jIvase martyAya |jyotiryachChantyajasram || 10.185.3

vAta A vAtu bheShajaM shambhu mayobhu no hR^ide |pra Na AyUMShi tAriShat || 10.186.1
uta vAta pitAsi na uta bhrAtota naH sakhA |sa no jIvAtave kR^idhi || 10.186.2
yadado vAta te gR^ihe.amR^itasya nidhirhitaH |tato no dehi jIvase || 10.186.3

prAgnaye vAchamIraya vR^iShabhAya kShitInAm |sa naH parShadati dviShaH || 10.187.1
yaH parasyAH parAvatastiro dhanvAtirochate |sa naH parShadati dviShaH || 10.187.2
yo rakShAMsi nijUrvati vR^iShA shukreNa shochiShA |sa naH parShadati dviShaH || 10.187.3
yo vishvAbhi vipashyati bhuvanA saM cha pashyati |sa naH parShadati dviShaH || 10.187.4
yo asya pAre rajasaH shukro agnirajAyata |sa naH parShadati dviShaH || 10.187.5

pra nUnaM jAtavedasamashvaM hinota vAjinam |idaM no barhirAsade || 10.188.1
asya pra jAtavedaso vipravIrasya mILhuShaH |mahImiyarmi suShTutim || 10.188.2
yA rucho jAtavedaso devatrA havyavAhanIH |tAbhirno yaj~naminvatu || 10.188.3

AyaM gauH pR^ishnirakramIdasadanmAtaraM puraH |pitaraM cha prayansvaH || 10.189.1
antashcharati rochanAsya prANAdapAnatI |vyakhyanmahiSho divam || 10.189.2
triMshaddhAma vi rAjati vAkpataMgAya dhIyate |prati vastoraha dyubhiH || 10.189.3

R^itaM cha satyaM chAbhIddhAttapaso.adhyajAyata |tato rAtryajAyata tataH samudro arNavaH || 10.190.1
samudrAdarNavAdadhi saMvatsaro ajAyata |ahorAtrANi vidadhadvishvasya miShato vashI || 10.190.2
sUryAchandramasau dhAtA yathApUrvamakalpayat |divaM cha pR^ithivIM chAntarikShamatho svaH || 10.190.3

saMsamidyuvase vR^iShannagne vishvAnyarya A |iLaspade samidhyase sa no vasUnyA bhara || 10.191.1
saM gachChadhvaM saM vadadhvaM saM vo manAMsi jAnatAm |devA bhAgaM yathA pUrve saMjAnAnA upAsate || 10.191.2
samAno mantraH samitiH samAnI samAnaM manaH saha chittameShAm |samAnaM mantramabhi mantraye vaH samAnena vo haviShA juhomi || 10.191.3
samAnI va AkUtiH samAnA hR^idayAni vaH |samAnamastu vo mano yathA vaH susahAsati || 10.191.4

##
Last updated July 2, 2013

Special mention : Initial processing and help by Avinash and Shashi Sathaye, 
Avinash Chopde, Shree Devi Kumar, Sunder Hattangadi, John Gardner.
Reprocessed from Original in final form by Detlef Eichler with additional corrections.
See Detlef's site http://www.detlef108.de/Rigveda.htm
for other details and formats.

The text is shown without accents (Anudattas, dependent Svaritas,
and independent Svaritas including Kampas). Words are connected (agnimILe). 
Ch is doubled as in gachChati according to the rules of Rigveda-Pratishakhya. 
At the end of a word m is replaced by Anusvara M if the initial letter of the
following word is a labial stop consonant (p, ph, b, bh, m).
Visarga H before sh, Sh or s followed by a voiceless consonant has been restored.

Source : The Aufrecht/van Nooten/Holland (Samhita) version
of the Rigveda (http://www.people.fas.harvard.edu/~witzel/onlineRV.htm).
In this text accented vowels have Udatta or 'independent Svarita' markers.
Kampas are not shown. Words are separated (agnim ILe). 
Ch is not doubled as in gaChati. At the end of a word we find m before
a following labial stop consonant (p, ph, b, bh, m).
Visarga H before sh, Sh or s followed by a voiceless consonant has 
been dropped according to a rule of  Rigveda-Pratishakhya.

Send corrections to   : detlefeichler@googlemail.com, sanskrit@cheerful.com

The text is to be used for personal studies and research only.
Any use for commercial purpose is prohibited as a `gentleman's' agreement.
